Expanding Strike Situation 30

Shops Closed, Transportation Cut Off

Barcelona - After 9:00 AM this morning, the strike situation suddenly expanded. All shops were closed, and public transportation was cut off. Only a few private cars and delivery trucks were running on the streets. Food shops and bakeries were half-open, allowing residents to enter and buy food. Crowds gathered on the streets, discussing the situation, but order was maintained. Suburban electric railways stopped running, while major railway lines operated almost as usual. Other cities in Catalonia also announced a general strike. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Madrid - The general strike in the capital has spread to various provincial towns by afternoon. The situation in Catalonia is particularly tense, with most telephone communication cut off. Unconfirmed reports indicate that fierce fighting has broken out in Seville and Barcelona. As of the time of the dispatch, 200 people have been arrested, more than 20 injured, and three dead. Unrest is growing. (National dispatch, 5th)

Madrid - Due to the strike in the capital, things are inconvenient. The purpose of the strike is to remove the three Catholic Party members from the new cabinet. The Spanish Republic is currently facing its most serious crisis since its establishment. A state of martial law has been declared in the province of Asturias due to riots, but the cabinet hopes that the capital will not need to be declared under siege. So far, no major riots have occurred in the capital. Only a few trams occasionally run on the streets, each guarded by four soldiers. Besides milk stalls, some tobacco shops and food stores are still open. Crowds are gathering outside bakeries, preemptively stocking up in case of a strike. A striker dressed in military uniform entered a camp trying to steal a machine gun but was discovered and arrested. Police also found a machine gun at the entrance to a large camp under control. All businesses in Barcelona have ceased operations, and the overall situation is very serious. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Madrid - The new Lerroux cabinet had just been formed when the general strike began at midnight. Rioters were secretly meeting somewhere when police raided them, seizing 14 submachine guns and many pistols. Militias exchanged fire with strikers on the streets, and extremists attacked a barracks, which was repelled by soldiers, resulting in one death. At 1:30 PM today, the President of the Regional Government, Companys, broadcast a speech via radio, urging the people to remain calm and stating that he is closely monitoring the development of the situation. He said that to more effectively defend the freedom and democracy of Catalonia, the people must strictly observe discipline. He also said that he would report to the public via radio every two hours from now on. Catalonia has completely gone on strike. The city of Sabadell has been controlled by syndicalists and left-wing Catalan youth, who are maintaining order in the city with weapons. Many cars have been confiscated, with the words "Emblem of the Revolutionary Army" written on them. The parliament of the Autonomous Region of Catalonia is scheduled to meet this afternoon, which is attracting widespread attention. Rumor has it that the government of Catalonia has drafted a declaration announcing Catalonia as a state within the Spanish Federal Republic. This declaration will be issued when the environment requires it. However, the reliability of this rumor needs to be verified. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Current Commentary

The Opium Policy Under the Rule of Pseudo-Organizations by Jing 36

Opium is planted in the four northeastern provinces. There are eighteen counties in Jilin, the Hingan Special District, and various places in Rehe Province. In Liaoning, there are several counties such as Changbai and Linjiang. The total cultivated area is over 65,000 hectares, and the harvest will exceed 1 million dan. Our country has suffered from opium for a long time. Since the Opium War, the import of foreign poisons has not been stopped. We are currently seeking methods of prohibition internationally. However, the puppet Manchukuo is planting opium on such a large scale not only to increase its income but also to harm China and plunge our nation into a state of no return.

The people of our country have gradually become aware, and many are voluntarily quitting opium. This is because personal economies are feeling increasingly depleted, and the stimulation of opium ultimately cannot match the depth of modern civilization. However, in our northern provinces, general life is simple, and there is almost no entertainment for the people. Therefore, they take advantage of this weakness to turn opium into morphine. Initially, it is sold very cheaply and is especially easy to consume. Therefore, "white powder" is very popular in Hebei, Suiyuan, Shanxi, and Henan provinces. The depth of the poisoning and the severity of the harm far exceed that of opium because opium is easier to quit. Once addicted to "white powder," it penetrates deep into the marrow and cannot be saved. After forcibly seizing our four northeastern provinces, they also know that the people of our area are unwilling to submit. The nature of our country's farmers, though inevitably accustomed to conservatism, has the special characteristic of enduring hardship and bearing heavy burdens. The Japanese deeply fear that our people will use this point to resist persistently. Therefore, after seizing the four provinces, they first opened up the opium ban, allowing general middle and lower-class members of society to consume it freely. At the same time, they set up various temptations in order to eliminate the activities of our country's people. In other words, it is to eliminate the resistance of our nation.

Does one not see Taiwan after being ruled by the Japanese? The reason why its people's resistance is limited to only appeals is due to the small land and sparse population, abundant local products, and people being content with the status quo. However, the anesthesia of opium, which causes local young people with potential to revolve in the smoke of cigarettes and extinguish their courage to move forward, is also a powerful factor. Recently, the large-scale planting of poppies in the Northeast is not only intended to poison the people of the four provinces. One will soon see them transported into the customs, leaving no clean land in Hebei and Shandong provinces, or even spreading to the markets of the Yangtze River basin. The strength of the former Indian earth merchants will serve as a model. This matter is a great disaster for the people of our country and a worry about leaving poison to future generations. Therefore, we should make the greatest determination for the future of the nation and the survival of the country and quickly implement the eradication of opium. We should pay special attention to the source of the four northeastern provinces.

The government is currently strictly prohibiting opium and repeatedly ordering people to quit on schedule. If it can persevere, the source of opium can be expected to gradually be cut off. However, this kind of opium disaster has been caused for a long time, and the source of the poison is deep. Relying only on the prohibition of laws may still not be enough to achieve absolute results. Therefore, moral self-control is also sufficient to supplement the shortcomings of the laws. Social power originates from the people. If various groups can persuade in many ways, first make those who have jobs quit opium to awaken the self-awareness of each individual, then those who are addicted will inevitably imitate and quit, and those who have not been addicted will never be stained. If we can refuse ourselves first, then even if people set traps in every way to harm our nation, what good will it do?

A List of the New Spanish Cabinet Members 37

Lerroux Appointed Prime Minister for the Third Time

The Catholic Party of the Center Occupies Three Seats

Madrid - The new Spanish cabinet was formed today, with Lerroux, the leader of the Radical Party, as Prime Minister, and former Prime Minister Samper as Minister of Foreign Affairs. The Radical Party occupies seven seats in the new cabinet, the Catholic Party three, and the Agrarian Party and the Liberal Democratic Party one each. This is the ninth new government since the overthrow of the monarchy. This is the third time Lerroux has served as Prime Minister. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Madrid - The Radical Party leader Lerroux has formed a cabinet. The official list is as follows:

Prime Minister: Lerroux; Foreign Affairs: Samper (former Prime Minister); Interior: Valgallo (new appointment); Army: Hidalgo (remains); Finance: Mela (remains); Agriculture: Ferrantes (new appointment); Industry and Commerce: Orozco (new appointment); Navy: Rocha (remains); Transportation: Yalon (new appointment); Education: Villalobos (new appointment); Justice: Esben (new appointment); Public Works: Site (former Minister of Transportation); Labor: Angelator Sollio (new appointment).

In addition, Romero (former Foreign Minister) and Treforasco were appointed as ministers without portfolio. After the cabinet list was announced, the General Labor Union immediately issued a general strike order. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

King of Yugoslavia Visits Paris 38

Barthou's Meeting and Discussion Results

Rescheduled Rome Trip Date

(Paris) - Political circles now acknowledge that Foreign Minister Barthou postponed his trip to Rome because he wanted to talk to King Alexander of Yugoslavia. The King of Yugoslavia departed from Belgrade last night and will arrive in Paris tomorrow. The King of Yugoslavia is traveling on the torpedo destroyer Dubrovnik along the Dalmatian coast. En route he will visit the island of Korcula. The French Mediterranean Fleet will escort him to Marseille. Paris regards the King of Yugoslavia's visit as a very important event, and its outcome will have a significant impact on Foreign Minister Barthou's future meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. (National dispatch, 5th)

(Paris) - The date of Foreign Minister Barthou's trip to Rome to meet with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is currently undetermined, but it is said that Barthou will not be able to go before All Saints' Day (i.e., November 1st). King Alexander of Yugoslavia is scheduled to visit France on the 9th of this month, and Barthou will definitely wait for him to come so that he can have the results of his talks with the King of Yugoslavia in preparation for his meeting with Mussolini. (Havas dispatch, 4th) - The capital of Yugoslavia - King Alexander and Queen Marie recently left here for the port of Zelenika in Dalmatia, from where they will travel by cruiser to France. Foreign Minister Yevtic is also traveling with them. According to Yevtic, speaking to a Havas reporter, the King's trip is a clear expression of Yugoslavia's feelings and sincerity towards France, and is enough to show that the friendship between the two countries is an unbreakable chain. He also said that after the King's visit to the Serbian capital, this trip further proves that France and Yugoslavia are cooperating in a harmonious way to solve the problems of consolidating peace and guaranteeing the interests of both countries. (National dispatch, 5th)

(Paris) - London newspapers report that French Foreign Minister Barthou's trip to Rome has been postponed, but this has not yet been officially confirmed here. However, according to reports from Rome, the news from London does not seem to be entirely unfounded. Political circles here also say that Barthou's postponement of his trip to Italy is probably due to the fact that the initial negotiations with the Italian side have not yet yielded satisfactory results. Therefore, Barthou believes that the time for a personal trip to Rome to negotiate directly with Mussolini is not yet ripe. Another thing to note is that the various conveniences that the French Foreign Ministry had planned to give to the Italian people in the Tunisian colony have now been objected to by the Ministry of Colonies, so the progress of the Foreign Ministry's negotiations has been hampered. In addition, Foreign Minister Barthou is not willing to rush to mediate the dispute between Italy and Yugoslavia. (National dispatch, 4th)

Austrian Socialist Party Conspiracy Exposed 39

Secret Code Commands Seized

Several Leaders Arrested

Vienna - Today, the public was shocked to discover a Socialist plot to start an uprising throughout the country. A messenger driving a car was arrested in the countryside of Floridsdorf, and many coded commands were seized. After decoding them, it was learned that they were detailed instructions for the Socialist Party to carry out a violent coup, including detailed locations for machine guns and where party members were to be ambushed. There was also a list of the current number of Red Front lines. According to their plans, they intended to start uprisings not only in Vienna but also in Innsbruck, Graz, and Linz. Many of the leaders mentioned in the list have been arrested by the police today, and many more will be arrested in the next few days. At the same time, the government has implemented various plans to deal with the incident. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Austrian Government Prepares to Return Private Property of the Royal Family 40

Vienna - The private property of the Habsburg royal family in Austria is now being returned by the Austrian government in consultation with the royal family. It is said that the government is willing to return various works of art, including the world-famous Vienna Museum, as well as two large estates, one small estate, four residences, five houses in Vienna, two royal palaces, and the royal treasures. However, the Hofburg Palace and Schönbrunn Palace, as well as the Crown Jewels, will remain state property. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

French Prime Minister's Broadcast Speech Explaining Constitutional Reform Plan 41

Said the Move Aims to Avoid Dictatorship

Foreign Policy Based on Peace

Hopes for People's Sincere Unity

(Paris) - Tonight, Prime Minister Doumergue gave his sixth broadcast speech explaining his plan to reform the constitution. He said that this kind of reform is to avoid the dictatorship of one or a few people, because the evolution from disorder to anarchy and ultimately to dictatorship is inevitable. The Prime Minister went on to say that he wanted to select officials in major institutions to be subordinate to the Prime Minister's Office. In this way, the Prime Minister can easily understand the affairs of the major departments and easily achieve the effect of full administrative cooperation. In addition to the General Secretariat, the Prime Minister's Office also has the Higher Committee of National Defense and the National Economic Council attached to it. The members of the National Economic Council are appointed by the government, and their authority is to provide advice to the government. Economic Committee sub-branches are also set up in various places to make their tasks easier to carry out. The Prime Minister went on to say that he wanted to completely separate political and judicial institutions and had already drafted a plan that would be submitted to Congress for discussion. Doumergue then described one by one the results that the government had achieved in various aspects, saying that they had been very effective. Doumergue said that in terms of foreign policy, the policy that the French government is determined to implement is to maintain peace to the greatest possible extent. France itself is actively promoting peace, and France is sincerely cooperating with all countries that have the same goal of peace. Finally, Doumergue criticized the unified front of the Socialist Party and the Communist Party, saying that its outcome would inevitably lead to dictatorship. This passage was very long. Doumergue concluded by urging the French people to unite sincerely, eliminate party prejudices, and said that since the constitutional reform plan has been determined, he will not be able to make any changes. He is quite confident that this reform proposal will be passed. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

British Conservative Party Conference Debates Indian Policy 42

(London) - At the Conservative Party Conference in Bristol today, Sir Croft spoke out against the government's Indian policy and proposed a resolution expressing his political views, believing that the union between Great Britain and India in the central government of the Indian Empire cannot be dissolved and urging the government not to approve any recommendations that could endanger the future of India in the Empire. The motion was then amended by a vote of 543 to 520. The amendment stated that for the benefit of the party, the conference should not pass any resolutions, especially because it had previously been decided that a special meeting of the party committee would be held when the report of the Joint Select Committee was published to consult with Baldwin. The previous meeting was very turbulent, with some making contemptuous noises, some making catcalls, and some cheering. The amendment was put to a show of hands. After it was passed, supporters of Croft's proposal demanded a vote and openly expressed their joy because it was passed by a very small majority. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(London) - The Privy Council met this morning. Mussolini Inspects Industrial Area 44

More Than 10,000 Farmers and Workers Line Up to Welcome Him

Milan - Prime Minister Mussolini arrived here today and will stay here for three days. After three days, Mussolini will tour northern Italy, the so-called Italian economic triangle, which includes the important towns of Milan, Turin, and Genoa with their banks, industries, and commerce. However, Mussolini also plans to visit other important places in the vicinity. Mussolini's trip will have significant implications for industrial development around Milan. Today, it is raining here, but many people still gathered at the station to welcome the Prime Minister after hearing of his arrival. Flags and colored lights were hung on both sides of the streets to show their welcome. After getting off the train, Mussolini passed through a 70-foot-high triumphal arch and drove into the park, where 15,000 farmers and Lombardy farmworkers, all dressed in local costumes, lined up to welcome him. Mussolini walked among them. During his time here, Mussolini will lay the foundation stone for a number of major construction projects and will visit major factories. He will also attend a meeting of 5,000 officers of the local Fascist militia, as well as a meeting of the provincial governors. On the last day, he will attend a grand rally in the world-famous Piazza del Duomo in front of the Milan Cathedral. (National dispatch, 4th)

Three Japanese Arrested for Plotting to Defraud Large Sums of Money 46

(Tianjin) - Three Japanese men, Taniguchi Isamu, Uematsu Karo, and Fujie Neno, were seeking employment in Beiping and studying Chinese at a fellow students association. Because they had not been employed for a long time, they had a whimsical idea and plotted to defraud a large sum of money from Chinese officials. The matter was discovered and the three were arrested by the Japanese military police. The three went to the headquarters of the Chinese military police in Beiping at the end of August, claiming that they had worked in the staff department of the Japanese military police headquarters in Changchun, but because the actions of Japanese officials and Manchurian officials were unreasonable, they decided to work hard for China and abandoned their posts to come to Beiping, requesting the Chinese Ministry of Finance to issue 100,000 yuan to implement their plan. Because their attitude was suspicious, the Chinese military police reported to the Beiping Military Branch and investigated the actions of the three men at the same time. Before long, the Japanese military police also learned of the matter and secretly investigated the actions of the three men. At the end of September, the military branch notified the military attache Shibayama of the details. The Japanese military police were ordered to arrest the three men and hand them over to the police of the embassy. The Japanese authorities ordered the three men to be expelled from Beiping because they had not committed a crime, but their actions were not cautious. (Japanese Associated Press dispatch, 5th)

Extortionate Taxes in Suiyuan Province 47

Decision to Abolish in Three Phases

(Beiping) - The decision has been made to abolish extortionate taxes in Suiyuan province in three phases, totaling eleven types. The first type and the second phase of five types have been completed. The third phase of five types is being prepared for abolition. After they have been completely abolished, the provincial government will reduce tax revenue by approximately 200,000 to 300,000 yuan per month. This does not include the counties. The counties have many extortionate and petty taxes. After an overall statistic is made, it must be reviewed and abolished. The bandit disaster in western Suiyuan has been suppressed. The remaining bandits of Yang Hou Xiaobian and a small number of those who fled have been scattered. (Special dispatch, 5th)

The Pseudo-Manchukuo Army Flees Towards Yutian Area 48

(Tianjin) At Wangjia Inn in Xifengdengwu Town, Tangshan, on the evening of the second, thirty-odd plainclothes strong men suddenly appeared, each equipped with a box cannon and carrying two large leather suitcases of bullets. They claimed to be a certain unit of the pseudo-Manchukuo army and had recruitment banners. On the third, they sent out two men to recruit along the streets. Three people, unaware of the situation, joined them. The town's self-defense corps sensed something was amiss and reported it to the county government, which dispatched thirty members of the San Nü'er River Self-Defense Corps to assist. On the morning of the fourth, the two self-defense corps surrounded Wangjia Inn. The bandits attempted to resist but were unsuccessful and were captured in their entirety. After being sent to the county, due to the involvement of a certain country, fearing it would stir up trouble, they were all expelled from the country. The pseudo-unit has fled towards Yutian Yahong Bridge. The provincial authorities, regarding the security of the Kailuan Five Mines, have decided to send personnel to investigate and reorganize. Mine officials and police will also carefully select capable personnel to effectively handle any incidents. (Fifth Day Special Dispatch)

They have ordered the competent special tax authorities to investigate the facts and appropriately reduce taxes, setting a time limit for selling them off. On the Eve of the Beiping Administrative Reorganization Conference 78

Various Committee Members Arrive in Beiping One After Another to Attend the Meeting

The List of Members of the War Zone Reorganization Committee Has Not Yet Been Finalized

Beiping Correspondence: The Fifth Conference of the Executive Yuan's Beiping Administrative Reorganization Committee is scheduled to be held tomorrow (the sixth). The administrative authorities of the five provinces and two municipalities, such as Shandong Chairman Han Fuqu and Chahar Chairman Song Zheyuan, have arrived in Beiping one after another. Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie is expected to arrive in Beiping at 8:19 AM this morning (the fifth). Suiyuan Chairman Fu Zuoyi is scheduled to arrive at Xizhimen Station at 8:00 AM this morning (the fifth). Hebei Chairman Yu Xuezhong originally intended to come to Beiping earlier, but was delayed due to the Gongyue Incident, negotiating with the Japanese in Tianjin. As of 1:00 PM today (the fifth), the 51st Army's office in Beiping has not yet received Yu's departure time. It is speculated that he will come to Beiping tonight (the fifth), which will not delay the meeting on tomorrow (the sixth). Shanxi Provincial Chairman Xu Yongchang may send a representative to attend if he cannot make it in time. Beiping Mayor Yuan Liang has prepared to attend as scheduled. Other committee members such as Zhang Lisheng, Zhou Zuomin, Jiang Menglin, Tang Erhe, Wang Shuhan, Zhang Boling, Qin Dechun, Wang Kemin, and He Qigong are expected to attend and participate, totaling about a dozen people.

The biggest goal of this conference is to build up morale. When Chairman Huang (Fu) took office last year at a time of crisis in the North, he declared that he had come to jump into a fire pit, working hard to stabilize morale. That work has now been completed. In order to further stabilize the North, Huang believes that it will be impossible to succeed without building up morale. Therefore, this meeting will have a thorough discussion on this point. The second goal is the war zone reorganization issue and the renewal of northern politics. Regarding war zone reorganization, namely the procedures for the establishment of the War Zone Reorganization Committee, the draft organizational law of the committee has been jointly drafted by Tong, Li Zeyi, Yin Rugeng, Tao Shangming, and others over the past half month, and was completed as of yesterday (the fourth). It can be submitted for discussion and passed at the conference tomorrow (the sixth), and the date of its establishment will be decided. After the establishment of the committee, it will be fully responsible for all post-war events in the war zone and will liaise with the Japanese to ensure their completion. As for the list of committee members, as far as this reporter knows, although it has been internally determined, before it is officially announced, any rumors can only be regarded as speculation and cannot be regarded as a fixed list. The renewal of northern politics is an inherent authority of the Administrative Reorganization Committee itself, and there is no doubt about it. Moreover, at a time when national crisis is on the rise, if we want to have diplomatic solutions and strength, the starting point is to improve politics. Therefore, Chairman Huang (Fu) has returned to the North this time with the greatest determination, working hard in this direction. Regarding the training of civil servants and the investigation of the political situation and public opinion of the five provinces and two municipalities under his jurisdiction, Huang intends to present his opinions at this meeting and discuss a method for promoting them.

The agenda for tomorrow's (the sixth) meeting was set by the committee's First Section yesterday (the fourth), and will be distributed to the attending committee members today (the fifth). Although there was a proposal to extend the meeting by one day, it has not been considered a concrete decision. However, there are too many reporting items, and a decision will be made based on the length of time available. Chairman Huang (Fu) decided to hold a banquet at the Diplomatic Building at 7:00 PM tonight (the fifth) to welcome the assembled committee members, during which the committee members will exchange views on tomorrow's (the sixth) meeting. (Fifth)

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price The London gold price today is 142 shillings and 4 pence, up a penny.

London Bar Silver Speculators bought in, causing the price to rise by 1.25. Spot price is 22 pence 625, futures price is 22 pence 75. Speculators sold when the price rose, and the market closed calmly.

Bombay Bar Silver The spot price in the Bombay silver market is 62 rupees and 4 annas, the November futures are 62 rupees and 5 annas, and the December futures are 63 rupees and 8 annas, all up 10 annas. The market sentiment is stable.

Exchange Rates: British-American The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning, with very little trading. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was 4 dollars, 92 cents, and 625, down 25. At noon, it fell 3125 to 4 dollars, 92 cents, and 3125. Trading became stagnant. This price did not change until 2:00 PM. Also, one US dollar is equivalent to 4 shillings and 0750 British pounds.

British-French The opening price was 74 francs 12, the same as yesterday's price. At 11:00 AM, it fell 9 points to 74 francs 12, and then rose 3 points to 74 francs 15. This price did not change until 2:00 PM.

New York Rubber opened lower by 8 to 12 points due to the movement in the London market, and then rebounded slightly. However, the market price fell by 7 to 11 points due to large-scale liquidation by various parties. Most were forward contracts.

The factors unfavorable to the market were (1) the lack of strong signs of trade recovery, which is disappointing, and (2) the panic selling of various stocks in California due to the political situation in that state, causing unrest. However, it is believed that this type of movement is now gradually subsiding. The securities market opened steadily this morning. Yesterday's upward trend still exists. Various quotations rose, at most by 1 point. The upward trend seems to be unfolding slightly, but there are no exciting developments elsewhere, so it is expected that the previous prices may not be able to continue to rise. Judging from today's atmosphere, the authorities' policy is turning towards stability and firmness. It is heard that the Reconstruction Administration is now considering abolishing the Blue Eagle and fixed price methods. The market prices of various New York securities are as follows:

Liang's Troops of the Sixth Route Army Occupy Taipingshan Shijingkeng 81

Engaged in Several Hand-to-Hand Battles, Occupying More Than Twenty Bandit Forts in a Row

The Pseudo-21st Division Launches a Full-Scale Counterattack but All Fail

Nanchang Correspondence: According to military sources, Liang's troops of the XX Division were the most forward line among the Sixth Route Army troops when they occupied Dajiaokeng Xiongling last time. According to recent reports, the bandits, seeing that the troops' advance was difficult to stop, dispatched the pseudo-21st Division to confront them. At dawn on the 28th of last month, Liang's troops began attacking Taipingshan Shijingkeng, more than ten miles south of Xiongling. The pseudo-21st Division defended tenaciously, relying on the dangerous terrain. After four hours of fierce fighting, our officers and soldiers became braver and more vigorous, launching fierce charges. The bandits were horrified and collapsed, falling off cliffs and into ravines, trampling on each other. Liang's troops captured more than twenty bandit forts in one go, completely occupying Taipingshan Shijingkeng. Afterwards, the bandit army, thinking that our army was either exhausted or negligent in defense after a great victory, launched a full-scale counterattack. Little did they know that Liang's troops had surplus courage and were very vigilant. They waited for them to pounce, calmly responding to the battle. After several hand-to-hand combats, the bandits were unsuccessful and fled in disarray, abandoning their armor and weapons. It is estimated that 300 to 400 bandits were killed in this battle, more than 30 bandits were captured, and one light machine gun, more than 30 rifles, two Mauser pistols, and a red flag were captured. (Third)

Relief for Peasant Households in Recovered Bandit Areas of Jiangxi 82

Forty-One Counties and Five Special Districts

Fifteen Yuan in Loans Proposed for Each Household

Nanchang Dispatch: The Rural Cooperative Committee is investigating the disaster situation in this province. The most severely affected areas include forty-one counties and five special districts. Based on the investigation results, a proposed estimate of the number of peasant households to be relieved and the amount of agricultural loans has been drafted. The estimate lists a total of 292,000 peasant households in need of relief, with a proposed minimum loan amount totaling 1.5 million yuan (the table is omitted). The explanation of the table is as follows: (1) The counties and districts listed in this table are those that have been ravaged by bandits for a long time, have suffered heavy losses, and are in urgent need of relief. (2) The total original population of each county is based on the figures obtained from the Ministry of Interior Affairs in the 17th year of the Republic [1928] and the Department of Civil Affairs in the 20th year of the Republic [1931]. (3) The columns for the estimated number of people needing relief and the estimated number of peasant households needing relief are based on the general figures obtained from the investigation of counties where the committee dispatched instructors to handle rural relief, and with careful estimates referencing the disaster reports of the Department of Public Security of the Department of Civil Affairs and other agencies over the years. However, the special districts are newly established by dividing existing counties, and their population cannot be investigated. Moreover, they have not been completely cleared of bandits, making on-site investigation even more difficult. Therefore, the population and number of households have not been reported. (4) The column for the amount of farmer loans calculated at fifteen yuan per household is based on the costs of cattle, farm tools, seeds, and food during the farming season, excluding land and housing. Each farm household, averaging four to five people, cultivates an average of ten mu [approximately 1.65 acres] of land. The capital required is at least as follows: half a head of cattle (i.e., two households share one head) costs about eighteen yuan, farm tools cost about fifteen yuan, seeds cost about three yuan, and four months of food and oil during the seeding period cost about twenty-four yuan. According to the above table, the total cost is sixty yuan. If it is assumed that four households share one head of cattle, and most of the farm tools can be saved, only four or five yuan need to be added. Half of the living expenses during the farming season can be earned through day labor or rough handicrafts, which requires another thirty yuan. Now, if we calculate an average supplement of half, then at least fifteen yuan is indispensable. Therefore, it is calculated at fifteen yuan. (5) The columns for the proposed grades and proposed minimum amounts are because the number of households needing relief in each county is by no means uniform. It is proposed to simplify the complex by using a progressive series, dividing them into eight grades, and the loan amounts are also progressively calculated into eight levels. Those with 1,500 to 2,500 households needing relief are classified as Grade Xin, 2,500 to 4,000 households as Grade Geng, 4,000 to 6,000 households as Grade Ji, 6,000 to 8,500 households as Grade Wu, 8,500 to 11,500 households as Grade Ding, 11,500 to 15,000 households as Grade Bing, 15,000 to 19,000 households as Grade Yi, and 19,000 to 23,500 households as Grade Jia. The proposed loan amounts are also calculated progressively according to the number of households. Those listed in Grade Xin receive a loan of 20,000 yuan, Grade Geng 25,000 yuan, Grade Ji 30,000 yuan, Grade Wu 35,000 yuan, Grade Ding 45,000 yuan, Grade Bing 60,000 yuan, Grade Yi 80,000 yuan, and Grade Jia 105,000 yuan. As for the special districts, all of which are newly established by dividing various counties, there is no independent population survey number. The number of peasant households needing relief and the grade of loan to be listed are not estimated. However, the jurisdictions are not very large, so it is temporarily assumed that they are at Grade Xin and the required farmer loan amount is estimated. Those originally belonging to a certain county that are incorporated will still be proportionately transferred from the total loan amount listed in the original county. Those originally belonging to a county that does not handle rural relief and has not listed any loan amounts will be separately determined to make up for it. For example, half of the jurisdiction of Cihua and Zhaoqiao Districts originally belonged to a county that did not list any loan amounts, so each is separately listed with a loan of 10,000 yuan.

Yangtze River National Products Tour (III) (Heng) 83

Arrived in Jiujiang on September 15th and stayed for one night. Then, took the Nanxun Road to Nanchang. The Nanxun Road was a notorious corrupt railway in the past. Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek was stationed in Nanchang, officials and dignitaries have traveled frequently, making transportation extremely important. Therefore, after the efforts of the Ministry of Railways, a express train runs every morning, and everyone must buy a full ticket. This order can be strictly followed, so the order is well-maintained. A slow train runs once in the afternoon, which is more crowded. When the train arrives at Niuhang Station, cross the Gan River to the distant provincial capital. The Railway Bureau is currently planning to build a river bridge, contracted by Shanghai Fook Kee Construction Company, which is expected to be completed in May next year. Then, travelers will have much more convenience. The first problem encountered by our group upon entering Jiangxi Province was the issue of exemption from donations. It is stipulated that all kinds of goods imported from Jiangxi are subject to the Bandit Suppression Rehabilitation Donation, with silk and satin subject to a donation of up to 10% of the price. The exhibits brought by our group are purely promotional in nature and are clearly different from general business. However, it must be resolved before the meeting. We requested the provincial authorities to exempt this donation in order to promote national products. Therefore, after arriving in Nanchang, we visited Cheng Baiyong, the Director of the Education Department, and had a very pleasant conversation. We learned that education in Jiangxi is now being handled smoothly. Cheng is an educator who has worked hard and struggled. He is simple and quiet in his life. Wherever he serves as an official, the education community is attracted to him. He was introduced to meet Gong Boxun, the Director of the Construction Department, and agreed to continue the discussion at the Municipal Committee at 8 o'clock the next morning. Yan [Gong] also serves as the chairman of the Municipal Committee, and the committee is actually a miniature version of the municipal government. The next morning, we arrived on time with a written statement and were assigned Xia, the section chief of the Second Division, to forward the document to the provincial government, requesting approval for exemption from donations. Huang, the section head, was also sent to visit Liu, the Secretary-General of the provincial government. As a result of the earnest discussion, we were granted permission to promote the products. The decline of China's silk industry is considered a serious problem by people across the country. Having obtained the approval of Chairman Xiong, the Bandit Suppression Rehabilitation Donation Bureau was designated to verify and release the goods. This shows the sincerity of the Jiangxi provincial authorities in maintaining national products, which is truly commendable. If the request for exemption from donations had followed the normal procedures, it would not have been completed in ten days. Now, it was handled quickly in just two days, which is even more pleasing. Under the leadership of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Chairman Xiong, the various agencies in Nanchang are constantly seeking a way out in hardship. They start working at 8 a.m., which is full of vigor. Huang Guangsheng, the director of the Public Security Bureau, is an old friend from Shanghai. He said that after arriving in Jiangxi for three years, he must return home at 8 or 9 p.m. every night, which shows the intensity of the work. The Nanchang police are very amiable and approachable. On the morning of the September 18th National Humiliation Day, at 11 a.m., they ordered the people of the city to stop working for three minutes to express their grief. At that time, I happened to be walking on the road and stopped to remain silent. I saw that the police were able to responsibly train the people. This method is more effective than posting slogans and shouting slogans.

Our group held a meeting in Nanchang, using the YMCA as the venue. More than 100 people attended, including administrative officials, representatives of the party headquarters, and guests from various agencies. The meeting lasted for five days, and the number of visitors reached more than 30,000. Many military and government officials visited. The government stipulates that during commemorative weeks, officials must wear blue robes and black jackets. Purchasers are often troubled by distinguishing whether they are national products. Now, seeing the beautiful silk blue robes and black jackets on display by the Meya Silk Company, they are all welcome and have become a common need among people in the agencies. The Nanchang National Products Promotion Association is the center of the Nanchang National Products Movement, gathering people from all walks of life into one place. They have done a lot of work to promote national products. The Nanchang Women's Association is also working hard to promote national products and is very concerned about the Shanghai Women's National Products Year Movement. The five words "Women's National Products Year" have a deep impression in the Nanchang women's community.

Nanchang is a famous city in Jiangxi. According to a survey by the Public Security Bureau in the 12th year of the Republic [1923], the city's population is 274,203. It controls the hub of the Gan River and uses the Nanxun Railway as an export line. Since the 16th year of the Republic [1927], it has become a military and political center. The market has prospered accordingly. In recent years, bandits and communists have infested various counties, and the wealth of the entire province has been concentrated in the provincial capital. The number of military and political personnel and consumers has increased significantly, and commerce has flourished. What is particularly satisfying is that there are very few inferior goods. For example, piece goods, which have the largest sales volume, have almost completely become a national product market, which is really rare. In terms of commodity sales, Meya silk and satin have long had a place in Nanchang. The fabrics of Hongxin Factory, the twill and drill of the Meiheng Textile Factory, the Ink Chrysanthemum brand socks of the China First Knitting Factory, the Five Harmony Goose brand health shirts, the enamelware of the China Enamel Factory, and the felt hats of the Huafu Factory are all selling well, adding color to the Shanghai national products industry. The banking industry is also showing a rising trend. The Bank of China was established the earliest. In addition, the Central, Shanghai National Products, and other banks have branches, and their business is very developed. Recently, the Jiaotong Bank and the Continental Bank are also planning to set up branches, which shows that the status of Nanchang has been determined by the Chinese financial community.

Completion of New Buildings for China and Jiaotong Banks in Changshu 84

The China Bank and Jiaotong Bank have been established in Changshu for nearly ten years, and their business has been extraordinarily developed. The two banks hold the power of the entire city's financial community. The Daonan Company built a new market in the city the year before last, purchasing the entire site of the old county government. In order to develop its business, Jiaotong Bank first purchased land from Daonan Company to build a new building, which began construction in May of last year. At the same time, the China Bank also purchased more than one mu [approximately 0.16 acres] of land opposite it and started construction at the same time. Now, the new buildings of both banks have been completed and stand tall, facing each other in the new Daonan Market. They have now been inspected and accepted separately. Jiaotong Bank has also scheduled the opening ceremony for the 11th of this month and will move into the new business premises. China Bank will move in during the last ten days of this month due to temporary delays. It is also reported that Zhang Gongquan of the Shanghai Head Office will come to Changshu to attend the ceremony. Following the example of the China and Jiaotong Banks, Jincheng Bank, Shiye Bank, and Tongyi Bank have also purchased land to build buildings. In the future, the Daonan New Market area will be like the Bund of Shanghai.

Addition of Farmers' Warehouses in Various Townships 85

This year's prolonged drought has caused a disaster, which has greatly affected the autumn harvest. In order to provide relief in case of emergency, the local authorities have organized an Agricultural Warehouse Management Committee to investigate the situation in various townships and establish agricultural warehouses, hoping that the villagers can have a place to obtain loans. Currently, in addition to the Farmers' Bank, which has established many branches in Dongtang City, Meili, Zhitang, Baimao, and other places, the County Management Committee is also setting up new warehouses based on the reports from various townships. However, the number of townships applying for additional warehouses is very large, and it is difficult to cope with due to limited funds. Based on actual observation, Hexing Town in Shazhou City and Liantang Town in the Third District are indeed necessary to establish. On the 4th of this month, the committee decided to first set up two places, and will continue to add more successively, and follow the provincial order to establish them within this month, so that farmers can store and mortgage goods.

Renovation of Tiger Hill Scenic Spot in Suzhou 86

Tiger Hill, a famous scenic spot in Suzhou, is currently being renovated by local people such as Zhang Yunbo, who are raising funds to renovate the scenery, bridges, and roads, and rebuild the Zhenzhuo Bridge. The work was completed on the 4th. The renovation of the Copper Bridge has also been completed. The construction of the Suzhou Chamber of Commerce Memorial Forest House at the foot of the mountain is scheduled for the Double Ninth Festival according to the lunar calendar. Currently, they are working on repairing the Tomb of the Five Men and the General Ge Temple, and building a standard clock on the Thousand-People Stone in the mountain. Finally, they are building a ring road around the mountain to connect to the ring road around the city, to facilitate foreign tourists.

Convening a Meeting of Six Counties to Unify Measuring Instruments 87

The measuring instruments in the counties south of the Yangtze River have always been inconsistent and varied. Now, according to the order to implement the new system, it is urgent to unify them. For this reason, County Magistrate Wu of this county has specifically scheduled a meeting of representatives from the county governments of Kunshan, Wujiang, Changzhou, Changshu, and Wuxi, as well as representatives from the grain industry of each county, at 2 p.m. on the 15th of this month to discuss the unification method, so that each county can implement it at the same time.

Anti-Smoking Association Begins Arresting Smokers 88

The Anti-Smoking Association of Wu County has now begun investigating unregistered smokers. Yesterday, two smokers, Ding Zhengfang and Gu A'si, were arrested and will be sent to the province for military law prosecution. A total of 14,024 smokers have been registered in the county and have been reported to the province for record yesterday. All smoker permits will be distributed within one or two hundred days, it is said.

Wuxi Doctor Injured in Drug Research Explosion 89

Zhang Jiabing, a famous throat doctor in Yuantong Road, Guangfu Gate, has a secret recipe. Even the most dangerous throat diseases can be cured by Zhang's treatment, so his business is excellent. In recent days, Zhang was preparing medicinal materials to make swelling-reducing pearl yellow powder, throat-protecting pearl yellow powder, and flesh-regenerating powder, etc. He used a huge grinding vat behind the clinic and had been grinding for two days. At 7:30 p.m. the night before, Zhang and his son Xijun and others were sitting around the dinner table, while the coachman A'er was grinding the medicinal materials. Suddenly, there was a loud bang in the grinding vat, and it exploded instantly, injuring A'er's eyes. The vest and trousers he was wearing were all burned. His flesh was a bloody mess and he was severely injured. The objects in the room and the glass in the windows were completely shattered. The grinding pestle and grinding vat were smashed to pieces and flew several feet away. Zhang's daughter-in-law Xiang Shi and Sun Lin Sheng were slightly injured. After the incident, the injured were rushed to the hospital for treatment, and the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau also sent police to the scene to investigate and summoned Zhang Jiabing to the bureau for questioning. However, the cause of the explosion is still unknown.

Solicitation of Shares for Wuxi-Shanghai Highway 90

Tu Xiaolai and Xu Peihuang came to Wuxi a few days ago to discuss the solicitation of shares with Director Yan and other preparatory directors and promoters. Then, they went to Chu to inspect the Wuxi-Chu section of the project. Regarding the issue of share solicitation, the county government has scheduled a meeting with local people in the next few days to coordinate and jointly solicit donations. The Chamber of Commerce also believes that this road starts from Wuxi, passes through Changshu, Taicang, Jiading, Nanxiang, Zhenru, and reaches Baoshan, with a total length of 140 kilometers. All the areas it passes through are rich areas south of the Yangtze River. It was previously ordered by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to solicit merchants to undertake the project, and it has been approved by the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Shanghai Municipal Government to sign an exclusive contract for passenger and freight transport for a period of 30 years. Compared with other investment projects, it has full guarantees. Yesterday, it has been announced to all industries to actively subscribe for shares.

County Committee Surveys Wasteland in the Rain 91

The disaster situation in the fields of each district of this county is different. The high fields have neither been transplanted with rice seedlings in time nor planted with drought-resistant crops, so there is no harvest at all. The flat and low fields have been transplanted with rice seedlings relying on human and mechanical power to pump water. However, during the rice heading stage, they were subjected to the white dew rain and insect damage, resulting in most of the rice heading but not bearing fruit, which has not been seen in decades. The harvest has been greatly reduced. The county government, in view of this, has followed the autumn survey method of the Jiangsu Department of Finance, taking the overall reduction of the county as the principle. Those that are completely wasteland can be reported in a special register for exemption. However, according to the reports from various districts, the disaster area is more than 300,000 mu [approximately 49,500 acres], accounting for 75% of the total acreage. But according to the actual situation, the disaster area in the county should be more than 500,000 mu [approximately 82,500 acres], accounting for two-fifths of the total acreage. However, farmers who report wasteland must go through the district grain clerks, and the district grain clerks, with their bad habits difficult to change, extort and demand a reporting fee of five or six jiao per mu. Therefore, some villagers are unwilling to report wasteland. Recently, the rain has been continuous, and the wasteland survey committee of this county has set off in the rain to investigate the villages. As of yesterday, the survey has been completed and will be reported to the county government for review. At the same time, the Department of Finance has appointed Ye Tiesheng as the wasteland survey committee member for this county and is expected to come to Wuxi for a review survey with the committee members of the Department of Civil Affairs and Construction within a few days.

Resolution of Changzhou Tobacco and Alcohol License Dispute 92

Tobacco and alcohol merchants in Wu County had a dispute with the tax bureau over the issue of license grades. The provincial bureau once sent a commissioner to Changzhou to investigate, but no solution was found. Recently, the Department of Finance sent Commissioner Huang Zhefu to Changzhou to investigate. On the afternoon of the 4th, a meeting of tobacco and alcohol merchants was convened at the County Chamber of Commerce to mediate. Sheng Jingfu, the representative of the County Party Department, and Dai Xizhi, the representative of the County Chamber of Commerce, participated. Zhu Jinzhang of the Tax Collection Office negotiated on the cigarette part. After the representatives made every effort to mediate, the cigarette industry resolved the issue by adding 20-30% to the original tax amount for both large and small businesses. The tobacco merchants and the tax bureau have agreed, and it can be said that it has come to an end. The alcohol merchants' problem is smaller and has not been discussed yet. It is planned to schedule another mediation session, which is generally not a problem. Commissioner Huang, with the results already achieved, left Changzhou for Wuxi today (the 5th).

Resignation of All District Chiefs in Changzhou 93

Wang Qingdong, the chief of the Eighth District of Wu County, recently caused two bandits, Yang Jinchuan and Tang Shenggeng, to escape due to the negligence of the militia in handling a bandit case. County Magistrate Hou Houzong suspected that he had accepted bribes to release them and placed District Chief Wang in the custody of the political police for several days. Upon hearing the news, the district chiefs, considering that this year's drought has caused a disaster, the bandits in the four villages are gradually increasing, and the winter defense is tight, the defense regiments have been ordered to be abolished long ago, and the public security branches have also been cancelled one after another, the local strength is empty, and the district offices have no equipment, jointly tendered their resignations on the 4th. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Hou released District Chief Wang Qingdong and retained the district chiefs, and summoned the district chiefs today (the 5th) for talks, advising them to dismiss their intention to resign.

Autumn Rain in Jiangyin Affects Autumn Harvest 94

The weather in this county was hot for three days, from the 28th to the 30th of last month, just like early summer. On the 1st of this month, there was a strong wind for a day, and it rained that night. To this day, the 4th, the autumn rain is continuous day and night. The early rice in the villages has been harvested, and the late rice is also reaching the harvest season, needing sunlight to absorb moisture, so that the grains can be stored for a long time. Now, the ripe grains are likely to be knocked down into the mud, scattered all over the fields. Those who harvest have already sprouted. If the weather does not clear up again, the impact on the autumn harvest will be very significant.

Haimen Petitions for Return of Confiscated Property 95

Pu Zhuping, the owner of the Zhongying Pharmacy in the county, was arrested by the Nantong District Security Command for transporting drugs and sentenced to death after interrogation, which was reported to the Nanchang Camp for approval. The county was ordered to confiscate the store's houses and goods. Now, Pu's wife, Shi, has been wandering outside after the confiscation, homeless, and the children are young and need to be raised, resulting in a difficult and miserable life. Yesterday, she specifically petitioned the county government to forward the petition to Commander Qi of the Nantong District, hoping that he would show mercy, open the net on one side, and approve the return of the property to support her life.

Nantong, Tongtai, Haiqi Industrial Police Force Reorganized into Security Team 96

The Tong, Bei, Haiqi Industrial Special Police Force is now under the Nantong District Security Command, according to the order of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office, and has been reorganized into the First and Second Battalions of the Jiangsu Provincial Industrial Security Team, under the supervision and command of the Nantong District Security Commander, with the main purpose of protecting various industrial companies. When there are bandit police near the company's location, they can also directly handle it.

Yangzhou Convenes Emergency Meeting for Labor Conscription for Guiding the Huai River 97

The Jiangdu County Government convened a meeting of the directors of the Construction and Public Security Bureaus and the district chiefs at 3 p.m. today (the 3rd) to discuss the emergency conscription of labor for guiding the Huai River. The chairman was County Magistrate Ma Zhenbang. The summary of the resolutions is as follows: (1) Conscript 5,000 laborers for guiding the Huai River. (This is the minimum number. According to the provincial order, 12 counties must conscript 160,000 laborers in one period. Now, excluding Jiangdu's 5,000 laborers, each of the other 11 counties should conscript more than 14,000 laborers.) Each district shall apportion the assigned number of laborers as follows: each of the five districts, namely the first, second, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts, shall apportion 556 people, and each of the four districts, namely the third, seventh, eighth, and ninth districts, shall apportion 555 people. Each district shall apportion the number of conscripted laborers according to the above-mentioned assigned number to each old governing township, and shall conscript the required number within the time limit. The old governing townships of each district shall conscript laborers from their respective jurisdictions according to the assigned number and shall not neglect it in the slightest, so as not to delay the work. The laborers conscripted for guiding the Huai River can dig at least two to three cubic meters of mud per day. Each cubic meter is calculated at 8 cents of silver, so each person can earn 16 to 24 cents of silver per day. In order to show compassion for the hard work, each old governing township shall raise funds locally to provide each person with living expenses of 6 to 8 yuan of silver per month, to show preferential treatment.

Bandit Injures Victim in Xiba Town, Qingjiang 98

A group of bandits suddenly arrived at the home of farmer Li Deyong in Dahekou, Xiba East Town, Third District of Huaiyin, on the night of the 2nd and looted it empty. Li Hongyu, Deyong's son, because he recognized the bandit Zhong Yanqi, was a little careless in his words and was stabbed by the bandit in several places, intending to kill him. Fortunately, he was not killed. After the bandits left, Deyong immediately went to the Second Branch of the Independent Defense to report the arrest. In addition to capturing Yanqi and three other bandits, they were handed over to the county government for legal action yesterday.

Hangzhou Teenage Military Officer Commits Suicide 99

Wang Peicheng, a 23-year-old from Shanghai, joined the Volunteer Army and fought against the Japanese army in the January 28th Incident in Shanghai. Later, he went to Fujian to serve in the military. He was discharged from his duties last year and returned home. He was ridiculed by his stepmother at home, so he came to Hangzhou to visit friends without success and ran out of money. Yesterday, he committed suicide by jumping into West Lake at Broken Bridge. Fortunately, he was rescued by the police on duty. After learning about the situation, he telegraphed Wang's family in Shanghai to come to Hangzhou to identify him.

Ningbo Yao Qitang Dike Salt Farmers Suffer Robbery 100

In the area of Qitangxia Gaojiadun, Yaojiashetou, Wangjiashetou, and Yangdingqiu, which are located at the intersection of the Fifth and Sixth Districts of Yuyao, the sea tide broke through the embankment due to heavy rain the day before yesterday. The water depth in the salt farmers' houses was one foot deep, and the situation was extremely critical. The salt farmers fled to Liutang overnight for help and immediately loaded more than 20 ships of mud to rush to block the side of Qitang. Fortunately, the embankment was not badly damaged, and the sea tide receded soon after, so they were able to turn the crisis into safety. However, the salt farmers had already lost more than a thousand gold [monetary unit].

Duanqiaotou Farmers Kill and Capture Bandits 101

Zhong Ruilin and Zhong Xingsheng, farmers in Duanqiaotou near Siduan Port in Yindong, lived next door to each other and were quite well-off. At about 12 p.m. the night before (2nd), a group of 13 or 14 bandits broke into their homes and robbed them. At about 1 a.m., the bandits used a customary cannon to demonstrate their power and escaped with their loot. The farmers heard that it was not a gun, so they beat gongs to gather people to chase and capture them. The bandits were outnumbered and one bandit was killed. The rest crossed the river and fled. However, the farmers still bravely pursued and captured another bandit, Zong Lin, and sent him to the Panhuoqiao Police Station for verification. However, according to Zhang's confession, he was a highway worker and was just passing by and was captured, not a bandit.

Hefei Shanghai Bank Sets Up Mortgage Loan Office in Hefei 102

County Magistrate Guo of Hefei, considering that there was no harvest in the autumn and the farmers in the four villages were cut off from their livelihoods, corresponded with the Nanjing Branch of the Shanghai Bank to request the bank to set up a farmer mortgage loan office in Hefei to provide relief. It has been matured and the bank has decided to invest 500,000 yuan for a trial period of two years. The location has been selected at the original site of the Dasheng Silk Shop in Gulou North, which has been undergoing major repairs and will be officially opened for business within a few days. Local public groups are currently discussing all mortgage loan methods, which is also a ray of hope for the countryside.

Letter of Correction 103

To the Editor:

Having recently read in your newspaper (September 27 issue) the article stating: "Reactionary elements are actively engaging in treacherous activities in the war zone. Furthermore, the 'Humane Loving Charity Society' has been established in Tangshan. The majority of its members are from the lowest classes and among the traitors who have joined is Geng Zixiang..." I was shocked beyond measure. After graduating from the Baoding Military Academy in the 11th year of the Republic [1922], I have been working diligently and have always behaved within the bounds of propriety. Last winter, I returned to my hometown to visit relatives and have been keeping to myself, not interfering in any matters. In January of this year, Director Zhao of the Tangshan Special Public Security Bureau hired me as a consultant. Apart from occasionally assisting with official duties, I have not participated in any local organizations or societies. Unexpectedly, your newspaper has now branded me as a traitor and included me in the Humane Loving Charity Society. This situation suggests that a villain is fabricating names in an attempt to frame me. As this concerns personal reputation, it cannot be allowed to be damaged by others. In addition to filing a report with the Tangshan Public Security Bureau, I request that you immediately issue a correction to prevent misleading rumors. This would be most convenient.

Sincerely,

Geng Zixiang, Consultant of the Tangshan Special Public Security Bureau

To Organize the Sino-American Trade Association

According to the *Shanghai Evening Post*, leading figures in Sino-American business circles in Shanghai, for the purpose of promoting Sino-American commercial relations, recently initiated the organization of a Sino-American Trade Association. The Chinese representatives were Zhang Jia'ao, Lin Kanghou, Yu Zuoting, Chen Guangfu, Chen Zeqing, and Mr. Guo, while the American representatives were Mr. Hall Paxton, General Manager of the Shanghai Power Company, Mr. Bassett, Manager of the British American Tobacco Company, Mr. Hume, Manager of Chase Bank, Mr. Corbett, Deputy General Manager of the Standard Oil Company, Mr. Baldwin, Deputy General Manager of Dollar Company, and Mr. Fessenden, President of the American Chamber of Commerce. Mr. Minor of the New York association will arrive in Shanghai next Tuesday to participate in the development work of the Shanghai association. Chinese Consul in New York Presents Six Proposals

National Product Manufacturers to Jointly Study with Various Organizations

However, Chinese goods are quite popular with Americans. He specifically proposed six methods for promoting national products in the United States, requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to forward them to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, instructing national product organizations across the country to pay close attention. Upon hearing this news, the national product industry in Shanghai believes that this is a unique opportunity to promote national products. They will jointly study promotion methods with various national product organizations and request the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to instruct the national industrial sector to join together to develop foreign markets.

Financial and Other Three Public Bonds Drawn Yesterday Morning for Principal Repayment 112

Total Principal Repaid: 1.16 Million Yuan

Demobilization Bond Payments Due by the End of the Month

The eleventh drawing for principal repayment of the 20th Year of the Republic Financial Short-Term Public Bonds, the fifth drawing for the 20th Year of the Republic Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Public Bonds, and the seventeenth drawing for the 18th Year of the Republic Demobilization Public Bonds were held at 10:00 AM yesterday at the Bankers' Association at 4 Hong Kong Road. More than 30 representatives from various sectors attended. The drawing was chaired by Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department. A total of ten draws were made, repaying a total of 1.16 million yuan in principal. All winning bonds, except for the demobilization bonds (which will be paid from the 31st of this month), will be paid by the Central, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and National Industrial Bank starting from the 15th of this month. Details are as follows:

Attending Representatives 113

Attendees yesterday included Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance; Wang Zhijing, Supervisor from the Auditing Department; Jin Runxiang from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Fan Jietang from the National Debt Fund Management Committee; Hu Bijiang from the Shanghai Banking Association; Chen Shengwu from the Shanghai Money Trade Association; Jin Wenyuan from the Central Bank (drawer); Zhu Qizhen from the Bank of China (drawer); Mao Rui from the Bank of Communications (drawer); He Xiaoyuan, Zong Boxuan, and Liang Yaozong (administrators); You Dunqi, Ji Juncai, and Fang Jingzhong (registrars); Wang Huaizhong, Dong Qizong, Ling Qixun, and Huang Meizhao (clerks); Gong Baozhen, Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian, and Xu Bangzheng (receptionists); Luo Huizong from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce; Pan Xingfu from the Beiping Chamber of Commerce; He Bingxian from the International Trade Bureau; Chen Hao Yi from the Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Public Bond Custody Committee; Lin Leming from the Inspector General of Customs; Song Ziliang from the Guodai Bank; Jin Wenwei from the Wing On Bank; Pan Yonghe from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; and Ju Zhijing from the First Special District Court, totaling over 30 people.

Chairman's Report 114

After performing the ritual, the chairman gave a report, stating that today is the day for the eleventh repayment of the principal of the 20th Year of the Republic Financial Short-Term Public Bonds, the fifth repayment of the principal of the 20th Year of the Republic Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Public Bonds, and the seventeenth repayment of the principal of the 18th Year of the Republic Demobilization Public Bonds. He expressed his pleasure at the attendance of all the guests for the viewing. The total issued amount of the 20th Year of the Republic Financial Short-Term Public Bonds was 80 million yuan. With the exception of the principal silver drawn for the first to tenth times, this time is the eleventh drawing, with a total of six draws, each draw being 80,000 yuan, totaling 480,000 yuan in principal silver, which is equivalent to 6/1000 of the total issued amount of the bond. Therefore, the method of drawing is to use the same last three digits of the numbers as the winning bonds. The total actual issued amount of the 20th Year of the Republic Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Public Bonds was 6 million yuan. With the exception of the principal silver drawn for the first to fourth times, this time is the fifth drawing, with a total of one draw, totaling 180,000 yuan in principal silver, which is equivalent to 3/100 of the total issued amount of the bond. Therefore, the method of drawing is to use the same last two digits of the numbers as the winning bonds. The total issued amount of the 18th Year of the Republic Demobilization Public Bonds was 50 million yuan. With the exception of the principal silver drawn for the first to sixteenth times, this time is the seventeenth drawing, with a total of one draw, totaling 500,000 yuan in principal silver, which is equivalent to 1/100 of the total issued amount of the bond. Therefore, the method of drawing is to use the same last two digits of the numbers as the winning bonds. The aforementioned three types of winning bonds, the 20th Year of the Republic Financial Short-Term Public Bonds and the 20th Year of the Republic Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Public Bonds, will be paid from the 15th of this month. The 18th Year of the Republic Demobilization Public Bonds will be paid from the 31st of this month. The silk industry bonds will be paid by the Central, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and National Industrial Bank. The remaining bonds will be paid by the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, along with the due interest. Payments will be made in national currency, regardless of the location. He requested the supervisor to check the drawing slips and the drawing slip ledgers for reporting the drawing.

Winning Numbers 115

After the chairman's report, the supervisor checked the drawing slips and the drawing slip ledgers, and then the drawing was conducted. The winning numbers are as follows: (1) Six of the 20th Year of the Republic Financial Short-Term Public Bonds: 209, 479, 564, 652, 872, 960. (2) Three of the 20th Year of the Republic Jiang-Zhe Silk Industry Public Bonds: 15, 23, 59. (3) One of the 18th Year of the Republic Demobilization Public Bonds: 57. All winning numbers will be announced on a placard and published in the newspaper by the Ministry of Finance for public information.
