Master Anqin Opened Altar Yesterday to Impart Dharma 117

Scheduled to Impart Dharma for Four Days to Broaden Buddhist Connections

To Leave Shanghai on the 9th for Hong Kong and then Enter Tibet via India

Pujing Lama Anqin Hutuktu arrived in Shanghai on the 3rd of this month and resided at the Buddhist Jingye Society on Hed Road. On the afternoon of the 4th, from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, he gave a lecture on the Hevajra Tantra. In response to the requests of lay Buddhists Wang Yiting, Tang Zhugong, Huang Hanzhi, Feng Yangshan, Wen Lanting, Li Yunshu, Qu Wenliu, and others from Buddhist organizations such as the Buddhist Jingye Society and the Chinese Buddhist Association, he opened an altar at the same society yesterday afternoon to impart the Dharma. The Dharma altar was set up in the Buddha hall on the second floor of the society, surrounded by yellow cloth. In the center of the altar was a Dharma seat covered with yellow cloth. Master Anqin sat cross-legged on it. Above the Dharma seat hung a horizontal banner with the black characters "The Dharma Wheel Turns Constantly" on yellow cloth. The arrangement was solemn. The Dharma will be imparted for a total of four days. The program is recorded as follows: The Hevajra Tantra on October 5th, the Guhyasamaja Tantra on the 6th, the Jnana-Vajra Tantra on the 7th, and the Avalokitesvara Dharma on the 8th. According to Anqin's translator, Mr. Wang, speaking to the *New News Agency* reporter, the first three Dharmas, according to the law, cannot be universally spread, so the number of people is limited. As for the Avalokitesvara Dharma on the 8th, all men, women, old, and young can receive the Dharma. However, they must register with the society in advance to broaden their Buddhist connections. It is also learned that after Master Anqin completes the Dharma imparting on the 8th, he has decided to take the Italian postal ship *Conte Verde* from Shanghai to Hong Kong on the 9th, then transfer to the *Tina Leis* liner to Calcutta, disembark, and enter Tibet via India to arrange for the Panchen Lama's return to Tibet and promote the Central government's intentions.

Yongping Rescues Chunhua 118

Two Ships Arrive in Shanghai One After the Other

Yongping Acts Righteously and Courageously

Chunhua Expresses Gratitude

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Fuzhou-bound liner *Yongping* arrived in Shanghai later than scheduled this time, as it assisted in the rescue of the *Chunhua*, which was of great importance in preventing over two hundred people on board from running out of food and water. The ship has now arrived in Shanghai. The report on the ship rescue is described below. Manager Yu Da's *Chunhua* ship ran aground outside Quanzhou. After more than sixty days, workers and technicians from the Hongchang Machinery Factory were dispatched by the Shanghai Insurance Association to assist in the rescue. On September 23rd, it was pulled out of the reef and sailed to the sea near Jiunanji Mountain, where Fujian and Zhejiang meet. The engine suddenly broke down and could not move. The sea was very rough, and the *Chunhua* was unable to move. It drifted at sea for four consecutive days. The food and fresh water prepared on board were only enough for two days. Unexpectedly, an accident occurred halfway, and it was stranded at sea for more than four days. Food and water were cut off. There were a total of more than two hundred people on board, who had been starving for a long time, and there was no water. They had to try to catch a little bit of rainwater to quench their thirst. Just when they were in a dangerous situation, the ship owner, Hengsheng, sent an electric distress signal from the ship, which was received by the *Yongping*. The *Yongping* ship owner, Tang Liquan, sailed his ship to Jiunanji Mountain to do his best to rescue. The first priority was for the *Yongping* to provide rice and fresh water to prevent more than two hundred people from becoming starving ghosts. Then, he used iron cables to tow it to Sanpan South Port near Pingyang outside Wenzhou. At the same time, he telegraphed Shanghai to send a ship to rescue it, so that the *Chunhua* was able to escape danger and return to Shanghai, thanks to the righteous and courageous assistance of the *Yongping* ship owner, Tang Liquan. The *Chunhua* has returned to Shanghai and is now under repair. After the *Yongping* arrived in Shanghai, it reported the situation to the general office, which was greatly praised by the bureau. All the more than two hundred people on board the *Chunhua* expressed their gratitude to Mr. Tang and requested the Northeast Shipping Company to issue a formal letter to thank the *Yongping* ship owner, Mr. Tang, and all the crew members.

According to *New News Agency*, the Yuda Shipping Company's *Chunhua* cargo ship, which sailed from Niuzhuang to Quanzhou, ran aground mid-way. It was subsequently rescued by the *Yongping* and towed back to Shanghai. The company yesterday reported the grounding incident to the Maritime Bureau. The *New News Agency* reporter obtained the original text as follows: At 5:40 PM on July 18th, fully loaded with bean cakes, it departed Niuzhuang for Yantai to continue loading cargo. On the 20th, it departed Yantai. It encountered great difficulties due to strong winds passing through Qingdao. On July 26th, at 1:00 PM, it anchored on the ocean surface of Quanzhou. The draft of the bow was nineteen feet and one inch. At 1:00 PM, the pilot led the ship to raise anchor and enter the port. Unexpectedly, it ran aground at Chongwu outside Quanzhou. The second hold and coal bunker of the bow immediately leaked. It immediately reversed and retreated and ran aground a second time. The wheels were also hit. At that time, the tide was very rapid. It hired many small boats to unload the cargo and sent troops to guard it because there were many bandits there. It sent a telegram to ask for help. On the 31st, it received a reply from Shanghai, asking it to wait for assistance. By August 7th, no one had come to help. It sent another telegram for help and ordered the crew not to leave their posts. On the 19th, the *Haian* ship and several steamships sailed from Xiamen to unload the cargo. On the 22nd, the rescue team of thirty-six people and the Shanghai Insurance Company also came together from Shanghai. The seawater in the hold was then extracted. By the 25th, the cargo had been completely unloaded. On the 27th, it encountered thieves, who were repelled by the military police. Fortunately, no accidents occurred. On September 5th, it encountered a hurricane and the anchor chain was broken. It immediately replaced it with another anchor. By the 14th, all the goods had been unloaded. By the 17th, the holes in the hold had also been repaired. On September 22nd, after leaving Quanzhou and traveling to longitude 24 degrees 17 minutes and latitude 121 degrees, it suddenly heard a loud noise. The machine was damaged and the wheel came off. It immediately dropped anchor. Several rockets were fired at night in the hope that other ships would come to rescue them, but the result was ineffective. The radio was also damaged. On September 24th, a civilian ship passed by, so Fei Shixing and Xiang Zhuang were sent by boat to the shore to telegraph Shanghai for help. The weather was bad, with strong winds and heavy rain. The passengers on board were very panicked. Fortunately, on September 27th, the *Yongping* ship sailed over and began towing. At 3:00 PM on September 30th, it safely arrived in Shanghai.

Xu Peihuang and Wang Xiaolai Return to Shanghai After Inspecting the Shanghai-Wuxi Highway 119

Since the Shanghai-Wuxi Highway was approved by the Shanghai and Jiangsu authorities after being submitted by Shanghai celebrities Du Yuesheng and Wang Xiaolai and others, preparations have been proceeding smoothly. Some time ago, Mayor Wu specially dispatched Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, along with Wang Xiaolai and others, to Wuxi, Changshu, and other places along the route to inspect the highway situation and to contact local gentry and merchants to continue raising funds. The work has now been completed, and they returned to Shanghai yesterday. It is reported that the results of this trip were very satisfactory. Once the funds from all parties have been collected, preparations can be made for the highway to be open to traffic.

Another Batch of Overseas Chinese Expelled from Japan Return Home 120

Plan to Seek Relief from Party and Government Organs Today

Eight People Still Detained in Japanese Police Station and Not Released

According to the *Daily News*, Japan expels our overseas Chinese compatriots using a method of piecemeal transportation to avoid the attention of our people. The previous two batches of those expelled and returned home numbered over a hundred people. Those who arrived in Shanghai yesterday were forced to leave at the end of last month and took the Japanese ship *Asama Maru*, arriving in Shanghai at 7:00 AM yesterday. They are still staying at the Lao Gongxin inn on the Bund, in extremely wretched condition. Most of them are small factory workers and hawkers, including Wu Wentian, Xu Baolian, Zhou Chengqi, Chen Ahai, Ma Jinji, Zhang Sanlai, Ma Zuofa, Sun Dianzhong, and Xu Zizhong, totaling ten people.

Petition Party and Government Authorities Today 121

Yesterday, according to Zhou Chengqi, an expelled overseas Chinese, speaking to a *Daily News* reporter, the Japanese expulsion of our overseas Chinese compatriots is not only devoid of any reason, but also too contemptuous of humanitarianism. The overseas Chinese compatriots who were expelled and returned home this time were beaten and kicked by Japanese police on the boats and trains, suffering greatly. After being forced to board the ship, the Japanese police confiscated all the remaining money that the overseas Chinese compatriots carried with them in their luggage. All of it was confiscated except for the money to purchase tickets. Therefore, when they arrived in Shanghai this morning, more than a dozen people were penniless. Fortunately, the owner of the Lao Gongxin inn, who is from the same hometown as many of the overseas Chinese compatriots, treated them well. However, those who have arrived here are unfamiliar with the place and their livelihood is precarious. They want to return to their hometowns, but they have no money for travel expenses. They plan to go to the City Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government two agencies tomorrow (i.e., today) to seek relief.

Eight People Still Detained by the Police Station 122

The Japanese government is quite concerned that the expulsion of overseas Chinese will be sensational, so it is using a cunning strategy of transporting them in succession. In addition to those who arrived in Shanghai today, there are still eight overseas Chinese compatriots who were detained by the Japanese police in the Minamisenju Police Station in Tokyo on the 27th of last month. They have not yet been released and have not been subjected to the same abuse. They may be expelled and returned home next time. The list is as follows: Wu Panbin, Pan Yipeng, Zhou Qinglu, Pan Linde, Lin Jinwen, Chen Zhenmin, Zhou Xiqin, and seven others. There is one other person whose name is unknown.

The Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory Dispute Thoroughly Investigated by Party and Government Authorities 123

All Departments' Work Completely Suspended

Second Special District Court Held Trial Yesterday

Labor Union and Association Both Request Impartial Judgment

The Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory at 1102 Xujiahui Road in the French Concession, at around 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, because the Rubber Industry Union of the Second District, organized by the factory workers, sent personnel to the factory to collect membership fees, the two sides had not yet agreed on the number of days and the location of the collection, resulting in interference from the factory side. A major conflict and violent incident occurred between labor and management. Xue Fuji of the factory and four detectives sent by the political department of the patrol were injured, and factory workers were also injured. After the French patrol heard the alarm, they immediately dispatched a large number of detectives to arrest Wang Diansheng, a Nanking native and director of the labor union who incited the assault, and took him back to the patrol station for investigation. The injured were sent to the hospital for treatment, and the factory immediately suspended work to await a legal resolution. The details were briefly reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is an investigation and record of the various news items yesterday:

All Work Suspended 124

According to *Da Gong She*, after the disturbance at the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory the day before yesterday due to preventing the union from collecting fees, the factory's accounting room and office were destroyed, and the factory's supplies were also in disarray. The factory believes that the workers gathered a crowd to cause trouble, causing significant losses to the factory. In addition to requesting the Party and government authorities to investigate the matter according to law, the factory announced yesterday that it would temporarily suspend work pending a resolution. The work of all departments, including the rubber bottom, face, lining, stripping, packaging, and cutting departments, was completely suspended. Many detectives were stationed at the factory entrance to prevent accidents. Although some workers went to work yesterday morning, they were all prevented from entering the factory.

Thorough Party and Government Investigation 125

According to *Da Gong She*, the Party and government authorities believe that the workers of the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory gathered a crowd to cause trouble, assaulted the manager, and destroyed the factory buildings, considering the situation to be serious. Tan Peiyan of the Third Section of the Social Bureau was dispatched to conduct a thorough investigation. Yesterday, Dai Youheng of the Civil Affairs Section of the City Party Headquarters went to various parties to investigate the truth. After completing the investigation, Mr. Dai drove to the Social Bureau in the central district of the city to exchange views with Tan Peiyan in order to report to the Standing Committee and find a way to deal with the situation to prevent the labor unrest from prolonging.

Continued Detention of Workers 126

According to *Da Gong She*, when the disturbance occurred the day before yesterday, Wang Diansheng, the director of the labor union, was immediately arrested by the French patrol and taken to the patrol station for detention. He was sent to the Second Special Court for trial yesterday morning. Many factory workers went to listen to the trial. The injured detectives identified workers Xu A'gen, Zhao Mohai, Ren A'lin, and Wu Jingxi as those who committed the assault on the spot. They were immediately arrested and detained for secret interrogation.

COURT HEARING 127

After Wang Dian Sheng was arrested, the police conducted a thorough investigation. Yesterday morning, Wang was escorted to the First Special District Court, Criminal Division 1, where Judge Xiong Hui Cui, along with Clerk Tao Zong Kan, presided over the trial. According to the police lawyer, Gu Shou Xi, the case's details were roughly as follows: The defendant, formerly a worker at the Da Zhong Hua Factory, was dismissed by the factory in May of this year for organizing a labor union. Out of the factory's 1,600 male and female workers, 200 strongly desired the remaining 1,400 to join the union, which they refused. Disputes arose, and the factory advised against forcing membership. The defendant, being a dismissed worker, returned to the factory without justification. Amidst a serious and chaotic situation, the police department, upon hearing the news, dispatched four detectives to maintain order. Because of the defendant's shout to "attack," a group of workers echoed the riot. At that time, five workers and four detectives were beaten and injured. When the defendant was arrested, he resisted fiercely and threw a teacup at his head, causing injury, which can be proven by factory employees. However, Mei Cai (transliteration), the head of the Bei Dang Road Police Station, personally led detectives to suppress the situation, firing several shots into the air to quell the disturbance. Today, three more workers involved in the violence were arrested, and the police are investigating. Based on the crimes of obstructing official duties and inciting injury under criminal law, the defendant is being prosecuted, and the court is requested to handle the matter according to the law. The court then summoned the plaintiff, Factory Owner Xue Fu Ji, who was represented by Lawyer Li Mo, who stated that Xue Fu Ji could not attend due to injuries, but the factory had also suffered losses and requested to file a civil lawsuit. The losses suffered had not yet been calculated clearly and requested temporarily reserving the right to do so. The judge then questioned the defendant, Wang Dian Sheng, who stated: He is 35 years old, from Nanjing, and was a former worker at the Da Zhong Hua Rubber Factory, where he worked for five years. He stopped working there in May of this year. Yesterday, he did not go to the factory. He and Yu Shao Qing, the secretary of the First District Rubber Union, were eating buns at a restaurant at the intersection of Wen Lin Road. At the Jin Ji Bridge, they met Zhang You Cai, Chen Yu Cheng, and Xue Jin He from the union, who said they were going to the factory to collect membership fees, and that Zhu Jin Sheng, a standing director, had reported to the city party headquarters, and Mr. Dai You Heng had mediated, and Manager Xue Fu Ji had agreed to put a table in the car workshop to collect money for three days, the fourth, fifth, and sixth. The membership fee was two jiao per worker, and non-members were not charged. The Second District Rubber Union was established at the end of last year, with only 800 members from the Da Zhong Hua workers. My dismissal issue has not yet been resolved, so I am still a member. Yesterday, male and female workers went to the city party headquarters to petition, and the party headquarters sent Mr. Ji to mediate. Because Mr. Ji called someone to accompany him, Zhang Wu Chang and I hired three rickshaws to go together. However, I was unconscious at the time and did not know how the injury to my face occurred. Later, I was arrested by detectives, etc. The court then summoned and questioned the injured police detectives. Detective No. 328 testified that yesterday afternoon, a little after one o'clock, the police station received a call from the Da Zhong Hua Rubber Factory, so they sent me to investigate the cause. When I arrived at the factory, I saw people hitting others with iron bars. I went to the accounting room, and someone shouted, "Don't run, attack! Kill them!" Because there were so many people, I couldn't see clearly. My head was broken, so I escaped. Detective No. 319 testified that the one shouting to attack was the defendant Wang Dian Sheng. Wang immediately denied shouting. Detective No. 332 testified that he was stationed at the factory. In the morning, the manager did not allow the union to set up a table to collect membership fees. Dai You Heng from the city party headquarters came and said that it could be placed temporarily, but not permanently. The manager then summoned Xue Jin He and others and questioned them. Xue and others said that nine out of ten unions want bloodshed, and they shouted and committed violence, using steel lasts and other objects as weapons, and attacked. The one who hit me was Pan De Bao, and the one who hit the people beside me was Yang Zhen Gui. I jumped out of the wall, and they shouted, "Down with the running dogs!" Detective No. 357 testified that the ones shouting and attacking were the defendant Wang Dian Sheng, etc. The judge also summoned Mei Cai Ge Liu, the head of the Bei Dang Road Police Station, and Deputy Head Ge La Di for questioning. After hearing the situation, because it was past noon, the court announced that the trial would continue at 2:00 PM. The four injured detectives returned to the hospital for treatment. At 2:15 PM, Judge Xiong continued the trial in Criminal Division 1. Witnesses Fang Zhen Hai, Zhang Jing Yang, Xue A Lin, Lu Xiang Gao, Yu Xing Hao, and others from the factory testified about being beaten. Guo Yao Qing, a Shandong native, the factory's security guard, also testified about the violent events. Finally, Detective No. 316 reported the circumstances of the defendant's arrest. Because the witnesses were not all present, the court adjourned the trial to 2:00 PM on the 15th and ordered the defendant to be held in custody. Before the court hearing this case that day, three workers with the surnames Zhang, Wu, and Xue, who were involved in the violence, came to the court, first went to the registration office to get admission tickets, and when they entered the First Court to listen, they were encountered by the detectives who were at the scene at that time, who immediately arrested them and took them back to the police station for investigation, waiting to be escorted to the court for trial today and merge the cases.

LABOR UNION DECLARATION 128

The Second District Rubber Industry Union issued a declaration yesterday regarding the Da Zhong Hua dispute, stating: Since our union held elections on September 23rd, although the time has been short, we have not dared to boast about reorganizing union affairs and harmonizing labor-management relations, but it can be said that the results have been remarkable. For example, repeated postings of notices, strict emphasis on union records, and letters advising the factory are numerous, which can be proven by the facts and cannot be completely erased. It is believed that those in charge of the factory, with their understanding, can also imagine this. The occurrence of this unfortunate incident was truly unexpected, but upon thorough investigation, one cannot help but feel sorry for the factory. The cause of this unfortunate incident was extremely minor. The next day, our union sent personnel to the factory to request convenience for the union to collect membership fees. Comrade Dai You Heng from the city party headquarters was present, and after discussions among the three parties, it was agreed that the factory would allocate the car workshop to set up a temporary office, to be implemented for three days from October 3rd to 5th. Our union members, upon hearing the report, unanimously believed that managers Xue and Wu were worthy of being called wise and capable, and their handling was appropriate. They were delighted that sincere cooperation could be expected. However, the unfortunate breach of trust was like a bolt from the blue. October 3rd was peaceful, but on the morning of the 4th, the factory removed the tables and chairs from the car workshop. When Qiu Guan Sheng, a director of our union, inquired about it, he was told that it was inconvenient in the morning and would wait until the afternoon. By the afternoon, the factory was straightforward and blunt, stating that it was impossible to deal with, and in an instant, detectives were secretly deployed. Thus, this unfortunate incident unfortunately began, with more than a dozen live rounds fired, threatening workers who had no weapons, intending to make the workplace, which workers rely on for their lives, a burial ground. After the injured workers fled the factory gate and petitioned the party headquarters, the factory even regarded passersby as workers, injuring Mr. Wang from Pu Dong, and arresting and injuring Wang Dian Sheng, a director of our union who had come with representatives from the party headquarters to investigate. Alas, when the city gate is breached, fish in the pond are affected. What are people to do? This is unbearable to hear. This is a brief account of the incident. For several years, our union members have believed that they have not only been without fault, but have also made great contributions. For example, the factory's capital has suddenly increased from 70,000 to 80,000 to 8 million in five or six years. When Manager Xue was detained by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation movement the year before last, all the male and female workers went to plead for his release. These are the major examples. As for the worsening labor-management relations in recent years, it is due to the factory's jealousy of workers organizing unions, reducing wages by 60%, arbitrarily dismissing and transferring workers, and raising the status of relatives, among other unfair actions. It is hoped that all circles will understand, base their judgments on facts, and make fair decisions. This is our earnest prayer. This declaration is hereby made.

COMPANY LETTER 129

A letter from the Da Zhong Hua Rubber Factory Company to this newspaper states: We respectfully inform you that a worker riot occurred at our factory on the afternoon of the 4th, and we have briefly described the situation. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 5th, we convened a temporary meeting of the board of directors and supervisors, and the following was resolved: (Above omitted) On October 4th, a group of workers prearranged to form a team, disrupting each department during working hours, coercing strikes, and plotting riots. We had no choice but to request protection from the French police. Before the detectives arrived at the factory, workers such as Zhang You Cai led more than a hundred workers, rushing out from inside, carrying weapons, hitting anyone they encountered, and destroying anything they saw. They disobeyed the detectives' attempts to stop them and instead surrounded and beat them. The detectives avoided them by entering the accounting room, but the rioters destroyed the accounting room. Manager Xue, eight employees, and detectives were all beaten and injured. Such wanton rioting clearly indicates prior organization and a separate background, with the intention of causing disturbance and creating a serious impact. However, the factory had reported to the city party headquarters and the social affairs bureau before and after the incident, requesting them to stop it in the hope of eliminating it. However, the incident was unexpected, and the factory has lost its guarantee. Under this violent coercion, it is difficult for the factory to reopen without complete and adequate guarantees. If it affects the branch factories or the raw material factory, we can only bear the pain of completely liquidating. Before there is a solution, the company will temporarily send personnel to oversee it. (Below omitted) The details of the incident are further elaborated to clarify the truth. Since the summer of this year, there has been a severe drought without rain, and rural areas have gone bankrupt, resulting in the company's galoshes being slow to sell and both goods and accounts being in trouble. Therefore, both the first and second factories stopped production for eighty days. Although work resumed on August 27th, sales have not been smooth, so reducing production is also a last resort. Soon after, more than 70 galoshes bottom workers working on piece rate in the first factory, including Qiu Guan Qing, requested an increase in work. We told them that they were not listening to dispatch and were unwilling to be reassigned to other departments. They could only wait for the increase in sales, and there was no other way. Therefore, at that time, we still planned to adjust several workers to other departments to make adjustments. However, Liu De Gui and others stated that a meeting must be held before a decision could be made. Unexpectedly, the next day, the labor union sent a letter that did not mention the adjustment to other departments, but insisted on restoring the previous work requirements. It can be seen that they were deliberately making things difficult for our factory. Recently, the stock has slightly sold, and the number of galoshes produced per day has increased from 2,000 pairs to about 6,000 pairs. The income of each worker has also increased accordingly, but their actions are still extremely arrogant. Therefore, we know that they are not purely for the issue of increasing income, but are actually intending to sabotage. Therefore, we reported to the party and government organs for thorough investigation, but the party and government have not yet made any statement. A week ago, more than 70 of them formed a team to harass the work places of each department. On the 3rd, it was even worse. We asked Mr. Dai You Heng of the Civil Mediation Section of the Party Department to come to the factory to persuade them. At that time, all three parties stated that they would no longer harass the work place. Unexpectedly, after Mr. Dai left, the harassment continued as before. On the morning of the 4th, they came to harass again. The factory told the Party Department, and Mr. Dai instructed the labor union representatives to go to the department to negotiate, but they refused. Xue Jin He, Huang Jin Sheng, Chen Yu Cheng, and others said that it would not stop until blood flowed. The situation was fierce. Then we saw Wang Dian Sheng, Qiu Guan Qing, and others watching outside rush in, gather the crowd, and each hold weapons to rush into the accounting room, hitting anyone they encountered and destroying anything they saw. The objects and windows in the accounting room were completely destroyed. For a time, men shouted and women cried, and the order was chaotic. The rioters, seeing that no one was interfering, did their best to commit violence, and each department suffered huge losses. When many patrol officers heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, they dispersed in a crowd and then went to Jin Ji Bridge to gather, forcibly pulling male and female workers to the city party headquarters to petition in the name of workers. This kind of riot did not occur when wages were less than five jiao per day, but occurred today when wages have reached more than six jiao per day. It is obvious that it was organized in advance and intended to destroy it, which is beyond doubt. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt and foreign goods are being dumped, the rubber industry is even more precarious. Our company is still trying to support it for the sake of the workers' livelihoods, but this part of the workers is so violent that the company is forced to this point and has no way to deal with it. We hope that you will investigate and uphold public opinion, and the future of national goods depends on it. Sincerely, Da Zhong Hua Rubber Factory Xing Ye Co., Ltd. October 5th.

THE BEAN AND RICE INDUSTRY CONTINUES TO PRESENT ITS VIEWS ON IMPROVING THE BROKERAGE TAX 134

Lists four items to request the Finance Bureau to handle flexibly

The Bean and Rice Industry Association believed that the new brokerage business rules and the detailed rules for the collection of brokerage tax in this city were difficult for various industries to implement. It sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce to convene a joint meeting of various brokerage industries to discuss remedial measures. The City Chamber of Commerce convened various industries for discussion on the 27th of last month. Four methods were discussed and resolved, and the original letter has been forwarded to the City Finance Bureau for flexible handling. The original text has been seen in yesterday's newspaper. It is learned that the association believes that there are still imperfections in the points discussed the day before yesterday, so it specially lists four items of opinions based on the special circumstances of the industry: (1) The business items of the bean and rice industry are extremely complicated. If each item of goods must have a certificate, there will be more than ten certificates. Those who are brokers cannot bear this major burden. Therefore, the association believes that the business items of the bean and rice industry should be summarized into three categories: A. Rice, B. Miscellaneous grains (including beans, wheat, and all other miscellaneous grains), C. Oils (including various oils and cakes made from their residues). When reporting for registration certificates, it should be limited to these three certificates at most. (2) When the brokerage obtains the certificate, it pays taxes first, and there is no need to provide a guarantee or pay a deposit separately. The joint meeting decided that the registration certificate should be certified and obtained on behalf of each industry association, which is the most appropriate method. However, the association believes that it should be further stated that anyone who registers the certificate and obtains it on behalf of each industry association will no longer need to provide a guarantee or pay a deposit separately. (3) The application form for obtaining the certificate originally set by the City Finance Bureau must state the annual turnover and brokerage income. The prosperity and decline of each brokerage business often changes with the prosperity and decline of the social economy and the smoothness of market transactions. There are monthly and yearly changes, so it is difficult to predict profit and loss. Moreover, those who obtain a long-term certificate will estimate the business situation within five years, and even sages cannot foresee it. Therefore, the association believes that it is difficult to fill in the above regulations. (4) The application form must also be attached with a photo of the brokerage. According to the brokerage is also one of the merchants. It has not been heard that other industries have paid and pasted photos to the official. Why is the brokerage discriminated against alone? Therefore, the association believes that merchants in various industries receive equal treatment from the government. It is not convenient to comply with the matter of brokerage households paying verification photos. It is heard that the above four opinions have been sent to the City Chamber of Commerce and forwarded to the City Finance Bureau, which is requested to allow flexible handling.

THE MINISTRY OF INDUSTRY'S SHANGHAI FISH MARKET IS SCHEDULED TO BE BUILT 136

Bidding will begin today, and the Ministry has already raised the funds

Including the latest equipment, it will be completed by next spring

Shen Shi News Agency reported that the preparation and construction of the fish market by the Ministry of Industry has been quite effective since the establishment of the preparatory committee and its active progress. Now all the plans and budgets have been approved by the central government, and bidding will be conducted today to prepare for construction. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency specifically inquired at the office of the preparatory committee yesterday. The construction of the fish market has long been planned, but it has not been implemented due to funding constraints. The funding was originally set at 1,671,000 yuan, which was reduced to 1 million yuan by the Central Political Committee, and the drawings were changed. Now all the plans are in place, and the Ministry of Industry has also raised the funds, so it was decided to start bidding today. The location has been surveyed at Zhou Jia Zui Island, Ding Hai Bridge, Yang Shu Pu, with a total area of ​​more than forty acres. After multiple consultations between the association and the landowners, they have agreed to lease it for use. The land is located along the Pu River, where the river water is deep and can accommodate a large number of fishing boats. This bidding is for the entire construction of the market, including (1) the fish market, (2) the warehouse, (4) the cold storage, etc. The estimated cost is about 500,000 yuan, which is designed by architect Xu Jingzhi. In addition, the floating bank is planned to be built by the Jiangnan Shipyard, and the cold storage machine is planned to be designed and ordered by the United Engineering Company. In addition to the entire building, there is also room for future expansion. This bidding will be closed in the middle of this month. After signing the contract, construction can be started at the beginning of next month. After a part of the market is completed, the cold storage equipment and radio will be added to preserve fresh fish and report on fish harvests and market prices. In addition, it is planned to add several transport steamships to tow fishing boats to Chongming Island and other places. It is said that the completion of the entire market will be no later than the middle of next spring.

ROBBERS ROB THE POST OFFICE 137

Everyone sending letters was driven away together

Approximately 300 yuan was robbed

The Xin Zha Road Post Office branch at 79 Xin Zha Road, Changsha Road, Public Concession, was at approximately 10:50 AM yesterday, when the staff was busy receiving and delivering mail, when three robbers suddenly broke in, speaking Shanghai dialect, each wearing blue-black silk long gowns, and holding pistols. First, everyone in the office who was delivering mail was ordered to leave the door. The letter senders, seeing this situation, all fled with their heads in their hands. One robber followed the crowd out and stood guard at the door. The two robbers inside raised their guns and entered the counter from under the counter door. First, they guarded the branch director, and then they monitored each staff member, not allowing them to make any noise or act. The staff members were unable to resist, so they had to let the robbers do what they wanted. They watched as the robbers first searched the money order counter, then robbed the stamp counter, and finally forced the branch director Luo to hand over the key to the silver cabinet. When one of the robbers was about to open the cabinet, he suddenly became anxious and fled outside. Another robber, thinking that the matter outside had been leaked, did not have time to open the lock, so he also took the key and fled with him. Therefore, the silver cabinet was not opened. After the robbers left the door, the staff members urgently used the telephone to report to the Xin Zha Police Station. The police station immediately dispatched detectives to rush to the scene, but the robbers had already fled far away. After inspecting the money order and stamp counters, the total loss was more than 298 yuan. The detectives inspected the scene and reported back to the police station, and then went out to pursue the robbers. The branch also immediately reported to the headquarters to request that someone be sent to investigate and arrest the robbers.

HU XI YUAN HOPES THAT THE CHINESE PEOPLE WILL PAY ATTENTION TO QINGDAO'S INDUSTRY 138

Transportation and products are suitable for handling industry

Do not only regard it as a summer resort and tourist area

Industrial tycoon Hu Xi Yuan recently returned to Shanghai from North China. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency specially visited Mr. Hu and asked about the recent situation of industry in North China. After a long conversation, he paid special attention to Qingdao's industry. Mr. Hu said that Qingdao was purely a military port during the German occupation, so there was absolutely no industry to speak of. Since our country took it back, it was changed to a commercial port, and citizens began to gradually promote industry. Although it has not yet reached the stage of development, the future is unlimited. Its workers are diligent, hard-working, and obedient to command, and the industrial raw materials are abundant. It is easier to start handling industry than in any other place in the country. The agricultural products of the area are cotton, tobacco leaves, peanuts, beef, and fruits, which are the most common. There are also marine products. The raw materials for glass are also very rich. The coal, which is indispensable in industry, is also very convenient to transport in Qingdao. The city has the Ji Lu Needle Factory and the Qingdao Stone Company, which are not available in this city, and especially the products of the Stone Company, such as marble, marble, and various beautiful stone materials for construction, are enough to defeat the imported goods worth tens of millions of yuan every year. In short, Qingdao's transportation, water conservancy, products, and folk customs are all suitable for the conditions for handling industry, and the security is very good and the climate is excellent. Since the loss of the four provinces, it has become the throat of North China and will surely become a very important industrial and commercial area in the country in the future. I hope that the Chinese people will no longer only regard Qingdao as a summer resort, ignore its industry and commerce, and sit back and let foreigners take the place of the authorities, and wait until they have developed their great power to the point where it is impossible to recover.

National Zhang Zhongjie Invents Peace Fire Extinguishing Grenade 140

Patent Application, Low Price

The Peace Industrial Factory, located at Heji Lane, North Zhejiang Road, Shanghai, manufactures various Peace fire extinguishers and all kinds of firefighting equipment. Due to their low price and good quality, they are well-received by all sectors. It is learned that Mr. Zhang Zhongjie, a technician at the factory, has recently invented a Peace fire extinguishing grenade. It is a glass vacuum containing liquefied carbon tetrachloride (CCl4). When encountering burning gasoline or alcohol, the grenade can be thrown into the fire at any intensity, immediately releasing carbon dioxide gas, completely extinguishing the fierce flames in an instant. After many tests, the results are excellent, making it a truly beneficial tool for fire prevention. Each unit is sold for only two yuan in national currency. It is reported that a patent application has been submitted to the Ministry of Industry. According to Mr. Zhu Binghai, a researcher at the Central Meteorological Institute, the climate this winter is expected to be drier and colder than last year. Therefore, the factory is now actively rushing to produce stock to meet the urgent needs of society.

Foreman of Guanghua Dyeing and Weaving Factory Assassinated 141

Thugs Break into Bedroom in the Middle of the Night

One Shot to the Chest, Severely Wounded

Guanghua Dyeing and Weaving Factory is located at No. 20, Liyuan Road, Luban Road, Nanshi. It has been established for fourteen years. There is a foreman named Ni A'er, 39 years old, from Tongzhou, who joined the factory as a worker when it first opened. Due to his years of service, he has risen to the position of foreman. He is also honest, so he is highly trusted by the factory. He currently earns a monthly salary of 30 yuan and is responsible for managing workers and directing all work. The factory even allowed Ni A'er to move his wife, Ms. Wu, and their three children into the factory workshop for his convenience in supervising the work. Unexpectedly, at about 2:30 AM yesterday morning, just as Ni A'er and his wife and children were sound asleep, three bandits, each armed with a pistol, pushed open the factory gate from behind the factory workshop and broke into Ni's bedroom. Without asking any questions, they fired a shot at Ni A'er's chest, who was asleep in bed. The bullet entered below the right nipple and exited from the right waist in the back, causing blood to gush out instantly. The assailants, seeing their goal achieved, immediately turned and fled. Ni's wife, Ms. Wu, was awakened by the gunshot. She saw her husband lying stiff in a pool of blood, barely breathing. She was terrified and cried out loudly. At the same time, other workers in the factory also rushed to the scene upon hearing the news. There was a commotion and much discussion. It was not until about 5 AM at dawn that an ambulance was called to take Ni to the Penglai Road Yuezhifu Hospital for treatment, accompanied by his elder brother, Yan Shaoshou, his uncle, Yan Haichun, and the deputy foreman, Ji A'tao. Due to excessive blood loss and severe injuries, he was then transported by car to the Baolong Hospital on Baker Road for treatment. However, since the case involved assassination, the hospital, as a matter of procedure, reported it to the Aivenyi Road Police Station, which dispatched detectives to investigate. After investigation, Yan Shaoshou and others were considered to be highly suspicious. The Municipal Public Security Bureau's Ximen Branch was immediately notified to dispatch police to arrest Yan Shaoshou and others and take them to the station for questioning. Meanwhile, they went to the scene of the incident to investigate and found a bullet head in Ni's bedroom, which they took back to the police station for examination. They are now investigating the details of the case in order to apprehend the assailants. However, based on the circumstances, it is likely that the assassination was motivated by revenge.

British Motorcyclist Runs Over and Kills Prostitute's Maid 143

Prostitute Declares Unwillingness to Claim the Body

Body Handed Over to Pushan Villa for Burial

Wang Huangshi, an old woman from Wuxi, 67 years old, was working as a maid at the home of prostitute Li Huifang at No. 42, Daqing Lane, Nanjing Road. At about 8 AM the day before yesterday, she was sent by her mistress to buy vegetables. While crossing Aiduya Road, intending to go from north to south across the road, a British man, Bo Jisi (transliteration), was speeding west on a motorcycle with license plate number 2058. He was unable to brake in time and knocked the old woman down. A police officer arrived and recorded the motorcycle number. He then notified the Laozha Police Station to send an ambulance. The injured woman was rushed to Renji Hospital for treatment, but she died soon after. The body was taken to the Philan Road Morgue. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Tang, appointed by the First Special District Court, arrived to examine the body. The British man, Bo Jisi, testified that he was 22 years old, resided in the French Concession, and worked at the Yipin Bank. On that day, he was riding his motorcycle, license number 2058, from west to east on Aiduya Road when the old woman suddenly crossed the road from north to south from the sidewalk. He only saw her when she was about two feet away, so he braked immediately, but it was too late. The brothel owner, Li Huifang, testified that she was 21 years old, from Wuxi, and worked as a prostitute. The deceased was her maid. Yesterday morning, she ordered her to go out to buy vegetables. She did not know that she had been hit by a car until someone told her. Her family members are all in her hometown. She has already written to notify them. She cannot claim the body on their behalf. After hearing the testimonies, Tang determined that the deceased, Wang Huangshi, was a female who died from injuries sustained after being hit by motorcycle number 2058. As there were no family members to claim the body, it was handed over to Pushan Villa for burial.

Xi Xiaoren Dies from Eating Pufferfish 144

Shen Shi Can Still Be Saved

Xi Xiaoren, a 36-year-old Chongming native residing at No. 28, Lane 1961, Bailinan Road, Shanghai West, made a living as a rickshaw puller. Yesterday at noon, he bought several pufferfish at a vegetable stall. He then went to the Shen Yongxing teahouse owned by his fellow villager, Shen Wenxuan, nearby. Shen's wife, Shi, cooked the pufferfish. Xi invited seven fellow rickshaw pullers to drink and eat together. Unexpectedly, at 2 PM, Xi Xiaoren suddenly felt excruciating abdominal pain, realizing he had been poisoned. His wife was about to find a doctor to treat him, but it was too late. He died at 2:30 PM. Unexpectedly, just as Xi died, Shen's wife, Shi (57 years old), also suddenly felt abdominal pain and was immediately taken by car to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road for treatment. According to the doctor, fortunately, the poison had not spread too deeply, and her life was not in danger.

Minutes of the General Meeting of the Transportation Industry Association 145

Re-election of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members

Delinquent Members Removed from Membership

The Shanghai Transportation Industry Association held its first re-election members' meeting at 10 AM yesterday at the South Railway Station Transportation Association sub-office. The temporary presidium consisted of Li Mulian, Shen Huibo, and Zhou Renqing. More than 140 members were present. Zhu Yakui represented the Municipal Party Department, Zhang Dafu represented the Social Affairs Bureau, and Yuan Hongjun represented the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Li Mulian and Shen Huiquan of the temporary presidium reported on the association's affairs. Representatives of the higher-level authorities delivered instructions. By drawing lots, the executive committee members Shen Huiquan, Zhang Shutang, Wang Zhaosun, Shen Jiefu, Qiang Zhijian, Chen Zhisun, and He Bingxiang, totaling seven people, and the supervisory committee members Gui Yanfang and Feng Yunchu, totaling two people, were removed. Immediately following the re-election by ballot, Zheng Bochang, Yao Songtang, Chen Zaixiong, Yan Zhongxian, Duan Jingsen, Fang Huanzhang, and Shi Yinpu were elected as executive committee members. Wang Fengsheng, Shen Jiusheng, Yu Zaiting, and Li Zuochen were elected as alternate executive committee members. Shen Huiquan and He Bingxiang were elected as supervisory committee members. Wang Zhaosun and Shen Jiefu were elected as alternate supervisory committee members. The following proposals were put forward: (1) Proposal to request the General Assembly to pass the industry regulations draft, passed by the General Assembly; (2) Proposal to organize an evaluation committee, passed in principle; (3) Proposal to abolish the north and south offices, resolved to approve the cancellation of the north office and the retention of the south office. The association will remain on Wenjianshi Road and need not be changed; (4) Proposal to ban the registration of the same industry and those who have not joined the association, resolved to submit a request to the competent authority for prohibition; (5) Proposal on how to save expenses, resolved to merge with the third proposal for discussion; (6) Proposal whether the membership qualifications of members of companies at the north and south stations will change if they move from south to north or from north to south, resolved that there is no need to discuss and this proposal is not established; (7) Proposal on industry exchange rates and association cost savings, resolved that the first point will be merged with the second point for discussion, and the second point will be merged with the third proposal for discussion; (8) Proposal on how to provide relief to those who unknowingly transport highly toxic substances and are unjustly involved in lawsuits, resolved to hand it over to the Executive Committee to submit to the higher-level authorities for relief; (9) Proposal on how to handle members who are in arrears with association dues, resolved that a deadline of three months will be given to clear the arrears, otherwise, a warning will be issued first, then the rights to enjoy the association's benefits will be suspended, and those who are in arrears for more than fifteen times will be removed from membership; (10) Proposal on unequal treatment of the same industry by the railway bureau, resolved to hand it over to the Executive Committee for handling. At 4 PM, the elected candidates took the oath of office and thanked the representatives. The meeting was adjourned with the ringing of a bell. It was already past 5 PM.

Departure of Chief Martin of the Shanghai Municipal Police 146

The colleagues of Mr. R.M.J. Martin, the Extra Chief and Prison Superintendent of the Shanghai Municipal Police, wrote an article to send him off as he was granted leave from the Municipal Council. The article reads, "Jiang Lang has a line, 'What dims the soul most is only parting.' Today, there is someone who will bid farewell to the Chinese and foreign society of Shanghai. Who is this person? It is none other than Mr. R.M.J. Martin, who has stayed in Shanghai for many years, has long served as a police chief, and holds the position of Extra Chief and Prison Superintendent. During the European War, he once joined the British Expeditionary Force as a captain. He has now been granted retirement by the Municipal Council. Since 1905, he came to Shanghai to assist in organizing and training the police force. His goal was to cultivate honest, brave, and efficient Chinese and foreign personnel. He is not only admired by his compatriots, but also has deep friendships with many Chinese people. Without a thorough knowledge of Chinese, how could he have achieved this? He is indeed the one who has the widest circle of friends and the most guests among Chinese and Westerners. Not only did he master Chinese himself, but he also paid close attention to the study of Chinese by Western personnel, as it is considered a matter of course in the Municipal Council's regulations for Westerners to read Chinese. As a person, he has received advanced training. He is cautious and decisive in handling matters, possessing the demeanor of Zhuge. Although he is strict with his subordinates, his colleagues all respect and love him. He has served in the Municipal Council for as long as twenty-nine years, rising through the ranks to his current position and repeatedly filling the vacancy of Chief. The Municipal Council is extremely pleased to have such a police chief. He is able to cope with difficult situations and handle them appropriately. These achievements are unmatched by any police chief. Otherwise, the results of cooperation with the Chinese authorities would not be as satisfactory as they are today. He has been awarded the First Class Medal of the Army, Navy, and Air Force by the National Government. Today's China is certainly not comparable to the past when awards were given out too liberally. It is certainly a great honor for a Westerner to receive this. Moreover, not only is his own hard work seen by the people of Shanghai, but he is also able to take into account the hopes of his colleagues for a satisfactory life. Because of his strong leadership of the Chinese, Western, Japanese, and Indian police, all the police officers, under his guidance, are able to devote themselves to their duties. These two points have enabled the public concession police force to achieve its highest efficiency. The duty of the police is to ensure the safety and security of society. The ability of the police to fulfill their duties is the honor of the police authorities. He has strengthened the material satisfaction of all police personnel, confirming that this is a basic condition for improving work efficiency. Now that he is about to leave, the various achievements he has made in the police force provide a model for those who succeed him to assist in the police affairs and build trust in all parties. This is a success of his career, and it also reveals his honor. Although he is leaving, because of his hard work, the public concession police force has made great achievements, and he can be content. On this day of sadness for both Chinese and Westerners, their only sincere wish for him is that his health may be boundless and his happiness may be boundless."

Remains to be Transported to Singapore for Burial

Chen Wulie, chairman of the Chinese Overseas Association, passed away in Shanghai. The Chinese Overseas Association and friends from all circles of Mr. Chen will hold a memorial service at 4 PM today at the Wanguo Funeral Parlor on Jiaozhou Road to commemorate him. Mr. Chen was one of the earliest and wealthiest residents in Hong Kong, and he was an advanced member of the Chinese Overseas Alliance. He had meritorious service in the revolutionary work and economic assistance. It is reported that Mr. Chen's remains will be transported to Singapore for burial.

The Murderer Wang Nengxiang in the Case of Li Minghui's Lover Being Assassinated is Transferred to Shanghai for Retrial 152

Defendant Wang Appeals to the Supreme Court, Ordered for Retrial

Testimony Conducted Yesterday, Waiting for Huang Shaotang for Further Testimony

On March 24th, 1932, at approximately 8 PM, a shooting occurred in the Shanguangdao area of Hong Kong, resulting in the death of Feng Deqian. It was later learned that Zheng Guoyou had instructed the rickshaw driver Liu Xing (also known as Ah Liu) to hire a killer to murder Feng Deqian because Feng Deqian had stolen his lover, the movie star Li Minghui. Liu then negotiated with Xu Yongchen, promising 2,000 yuan for the job. Xu Yongchen then negotiated with Wang Nengxiang, who agreed. That evening, when Feng Deqian and Li Minghui went out for a walk, Wang shot and killed Feng. The above information was provided by Xu Yongchen in the Hong Kong court, and Li Minghui testified that she witnessed the assailant wearing a coffee-colored suit, which was similar to the color of the suits Wang Nengxiang usually wore. Later, the Hong Kong Police Bureau gave Wang Nengxiang's photo to witnesses Ye Youtian, Jiang Jiamou, and Zhang Kunyuan for identification. They all confirmed that the photo was indeed Wang Nengxiang. After Wang Nengxiang was arrested, he was interrogated and sentenced by the First Special District Court. He refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Jiangsu High Second Branch Court. On August 3rd, 1933, the Second Instance sentenced him to life imprisonment. Wang still refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Supreme Court. As a result, the original sentence was revoked and remanded to the Jiangsu High Second Branch Court for retrial. Due to jurisdictional issues, Wang Nengxiang was transferred to the Nanshi District Court for investigation, which concluded and charged the criminal court, requesting a public trial. The defendant Wang Nengxiang hired lawyer Pan Zhe to defend him. Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, Judge Sun Jikang specially opened the Fifth Court for the trial. Defendant Wang Nengxiang was brought to the court. He stated that he was 29 years old, from Nantong, and worked as a carpenter. (Question) When did you go to Hong Kong? (Answer) I went to Hong Kong in 1929. (Question) When did you come back? (Answer) I came back at the end of the fourth lunar month of 1931. (Question) Do you know Xu Yongchen? (Answer) No, I don't know him. (Question) Did you stay at the Jintan Hotel on March 8th, 1931? (Answer) No. (Question) Do you know Liu Xing, Zheng Guoyou's rickshaw driver? (Answer) No, I don't know him. (Question) Did Xu Yongchen give you 50 yuan and a pistol in the Hong Kong court and tell you to kill Feng Deqian? (Answer) I don't know him, so how could this have happened? (Question) Zhang Kunyuan followed you to Shanghai and arrested you? (Answer) I was really wronged. (Question) Do you have a Western suit? (Answer) Yes, the color is red and black. (Question) The official said, then that's right. The assailant was wearing a brown suit, which is similar to the color you said. Moreover, Xu Yongchen said you shot the gun in the Hong Kong court, and Li Minghui also said it very clearly in the Special District Court. (Answer) I was really wronged, because most people in Hong Kong wear Western suits. (Question) Where were you at the time? (Answer) I went to the Guangdong Dadong Company from Hong Kong on February 10th, 1932, and returned to Hong Kong on March 2nd. I stayed in the Dadong Company factory in Guangzhou every night, and Mao Er, who was in the same room, can prove it. Huang Shaotang can also prove it. (Question) Do you have any rebuttal evidence to present? (Answer) Because the Dadong Company has already closed down, the Special District Court went to investigate, but there were no results. (Question) Where are Mao Er and Huang Shaotang now? (Answer) I don't know. At this point, lawyer Pan Zhe stood up and said, "Please adjourn the court for two weeks. It has now been found that the witness Mao Er's whereabouts are unknown. However, Huang Shaotang's father is in Shanghai. It is said that Huang Shaotang has returned to his hometown. After verifying Huang's address, a subpoena will be submitted to the court to summon him to court to testify and exonerate the innocent." (Question) The official approved it. He instructed lawyer Pan to quickly investigate where Huang Shaotang is actually located and inform the court so that a verdict can be made as soon as possible. After the instructions were given, the court adjourned. Wang Nengxiang was ordered to remain in custody pending further instructions.

Central News Agency reports that the Shanghai Postal Administration issued a notice yesterday stating that the bureau needs to recruit postal workers. Electric Silk Weaving Factory Guild Praises Da Xin Silk and Satin Bureau 158

Since its opening, Da Xin National Silk and Satin Bureau at the intersection of Third Avenue and Shilu Road has been very popular among ladies from all walks of life. Therefore, despite the recent days of cloudy and rainy weather, customers have been crowding the store, which is very different from the past. This shows the enthusiasm of the Chinese people for patriotic goods after the national crisis. The Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Guild believes that the bureau's shift in business strategy has a spirit of commercial revolution and has already sent a letter of praise. Yesterday, the Shanghai Electric Yarn Weaving Factory Guild also followed up with a letter to the bureau, expressing its support, and expressing its outrage at the common practice of salespeople using fine domestic silk and satin to pass off as foreign goods. The original letter stated: "Respected Bureau, your adoption of a plan to fully promote domestic silk and satin in order to assist the government's policy of production to save the country not only provides effective relief for our country's declining silk industry but also allows our guild members, who are working hard, to have a place to stand tall. Our guild members, in view of the import and dumping of foreign goods, do their best to study the patterns, materials, costs, and prices in order to resist. As a result, the exquisiteness of many domestic silk and satin is comparable to foreign goods, and the price is lower than that of foreign goods that must be subject to tariffs. However, salespeople in the market do not promote them and use the psychology of the Chinese people's fondness for foreign goods to pass off fine domestic goods as foreign goods, which undermines the achievements of our members' efforts. It is extremely distressing. Fortunately, your bureau has risen up and built a new base for domestic silk and satin, which will surely wash away the shame of passing off fine domestic products as foreign goods and encourage our guild members to continue their efforts. In addition to our gratitude, we hereby send this letter to express our thanks and express our willingness to do our best to support the implementation of your plan."

Wuxi Opium Smokers Flee to Shanghai 159

Since the Wuxi Anti-Smoking Association issued a notice requiring opium smokers to register by September 30, most opium smokers in Wuxi have complied and registered. The fee for a Class A license is six yuan, and the fee for a Class B license is six cents. Those who register receive a receipt. However, in view of the fact that sales and smoking places and official opium shops have not yet been established, opium smokers still go to the original opium dens to smoke. Unexpectedly, at about 4 pm on the 3rd of this month, the Wuxi Public Security Bureau secretly dispatched a large number of policemen to arrest all opium dens inside and outside the city. Most opium smokers carried receipts from the Anti-Smoking Association, but they were all caught. Therefore, in the past two days, all opium smokers who escaped the net in Wuxi have boarded the Beijing-Shanghai train and fled to Shanghai in a state of extreme embarrassment. They are now discussing countermeasures.

Zhou Guansan Countersues His Wife 160

Demanding a Divorce

Zhou Guansan, the Chinese general manager of the Far East Aircraft Company and a native of Hangzhou, was recently sued in the First Special Court by his wife, Wang Yuqing, represented by lawyer Le Junying, requesting cohabitation and payment of 30,000 yuan in alimony. The details of the trial have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhang Qinglan of the First Special Court summoned Zhou Guansan, accompanied by lawyer Zhang Li, to the Fourth Civil Court. Lawyer Zhang stated that the defendant had filed a statement with the court today in response to the plaintiff's lawsuit, and filed a countersuit demanding a divorce. The lawyer also stated that the court had instructed him to advise both parties to reconcile, but this matter could not be carried out due to the bad relations between the two parties. Lawyer Le also stated that he had telegraphed Lawyer Zhang, asking the defendant to pay attention to the feelings of a decade of marriage and reconcile, but the reply was not only that reconciliation was impossible, but also that a countersuit would be filed, so no negotiations could be held. Judge Zhang then advised Zhou Guansan to reconcile, but Zhou stated that there was no possibility of reconciliation. The court believed that the defendant's countersuit was related to the plaintiff's lawsuit, and the defendant's countersuit had just been submitted today and had not been delivered to the plaintiff, so the case could not be debated today. It was ordered that the hearing be postponed to 3:30 pm one week later.

Harmonious Labor-Management Relations Lead to Thriving Business

His carving follows the Qin and Han dynasties and is not limited to the Zhejiang and Anhui schools. It is recently heard that to expand his circle of ink friends, he has specially reduced the price. After the deadline, the price for carving a seal is one yuan per character, and the price for writing a fan page is two yuan. Those who want to obtain Mr. Lu's works can directly contact Mr. Lu himself at the Liangzi Hygiene Class, 527 Old Baz Road.

The Original Script of Hong Lou Chun Shen: The script of Hong Lou Chun Shen, which is being screened at Carlton Grand Theater today, is the script of Hong Lou Chun Shen produced by Tianyi Company and starring Chen Yumei. It is adapted from Kikuchi Kan's "Wedding Duet," a literary authority in Japan. This script depicts two unhappy marriages, writing about a pair of resentful men and women who play a symphony of all kinds of sorrows and pains because of a very subtle misunderstanding. This script was published daily in the "Mainichi Shimbun," which was the most widely circulated in Japan. Later, when the single edition was published, it caused a sensation in the Japanese literary world and was made into a movie by "Tokyo Electric Power Co., Ltd." When it was screened, it was full of people every day, which can be called an unprecedented grand occasion. Now the play has been completed by Tianyi Company and renamed Hong Lou Chun Shen. The script was translated by the famous writer Haoran from Changcheng Bookstore, 47 Ningbo Road, Shanghai, and is still named "Wedding Duet." It has been published. Those who want to see the movie Hong Lou Chun Shen must first read the original script of Hong Lou Chun Shen, "Wedding Duet." It is especially suitable for those who love literature and art. The actual price is eight cents, and it is sold by major bookstores in the city and abroad, and Carlton Grand Theater.

Weather Report 172

According to the weather forecast from the Xujiahui Observatory at 4:30 PM yesterday, the weather in the Shandong area is cloudy then clearing, with northeast winds. In the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, the sky is overcast and gradually clouding over, with intermittent drizzle. The wind is from the northeast to the east. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the East China Sea have strong northeast winds. The Taiwan Strait has rain and strong northeast winds. The weather around the Dongsha Islands is very bad due to a hurricane moving northwest-west or northwest. The center of the hurricane, at 6:00 AM, had progressed to within 60 miles of the intersection of 19 degrees north latitude and 117 degrees 30 minutes east longitude. The wind force is very strong. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in Shanghai was a maximum of 68.5 and a minimum of 62.1. On the same day last year, the maximum was 83.1 and the minimum was 70.2.

International Walking Race Suddenly Announced to be Discontinued, Dissolved, and Reorganized to Continue 187

Date Set for December 16th

Route the Same as Before

Yesterday, the International Walking Race Association held its annual meeting at the Shanghai Engineering Association on Sichuan Road. Westerners Lee Ted, McKenna, Howatt, Ross, Izzet, and Chinese Shen Siliang, Shi Youhui, Zhou Yuyu, and others, as well as many other foreigners, attended the meeting. The outcome was unexpected. Many people had already made contact beforehand, leading to a chorus of agreement to stop holding the event. Our country had heard this news early on, so it strongly opposed the decision and insisted on continuing the event. However, the foreigners, given that no British people were participating and that the Chinese had won the championship for six consecutive sessions, made various excuses and refused to hold the event any longer, abandoning over thirty years of long history. This can be described as painful. After the meeting, American Howatt, British Ross, French Izzet, and Chinese Shi Youhui and others held an emergency meeting at 83 Central Road to discuss how to deal with the situation. They unanimously agreed to reorganize a Chinese-foreign committee, with an equal number of members from each side, to continue holding the event. The date was set for December 16th. The route will be the same as before. All Shanghai Chinese open walking races may be expanded to include international participants, and the scheduled date may be postponed. The Chinese Walking Race Association is scheduled to continue practicing the 13-mile race at 7:00 AM tomorrow. Those who wish to join should gather at the Tongfu Road intersection on time. Each competitor must hire their own lead runner to facilitate forward progress.

Women's class: Quarterly fee of 10 yuan (three times a week). (4) Term: From November 1st, 1934 to the end of April, 1935. (5) Time: Determined separately according to the convenience of each party. Notice: All those who come to join must first pass a physical examination before they can swim.

Municipal Stadium Preparing to Organize a Fun and Rich Ping Pong Competition 196

The Municipal No. 1 Stadium is now preparing to organize the second ping pong competition. In addition to those whose profession is sports, all ping pong teams from all walks of life can register to participate. The registration period is from the 14th of this month to the 4th of next month. The method is quite different from ordinary ping pong competitions, as its purpose is purely to promote indoor sports and increase the interest of the participants. The main points are recorded below: (1) Each team registers 10 players (7 or more, less than 10 is also acceptable, each person cannot join two teams). Seven players will be on the court for the competition. When registering, the number of each player must be clearly indicated, and a six-inch photo of all players must be attached, also indicating the number. The first seven numbers are the official players, and the numbers below seven are the reserves. Each game will follow this numbering, from front to back, in order, and no other roster can be arranged to change the order in an attempt to win by skill. If an official player is absent due to an event, the reserve player's replacement must also follow the numbering, from front to back, without chaos. (2) Competition method: using the continuous capture system. The method depends on the number of participating teams, drawing lots to divide into several groups. Each group will conduct a single round-robin tournament. After the competition, the winning team will be given a championship. This is the first round of the competition. Then, the winning teams will withdraw, and the teams in each group will be mixed and re-drawed to form groups to hold the second round of the competition. The winning teams in each group will still be given championships. Then, the winning teams will withdraw, and the above method will be used to re-draw lots to form groups to hold the third round of the competition. The winning teams in each group will still be given championships. The number of rounds of competition depends on the number of participating teams. (3) Each individual competition will use the best-of-five format. In each game, the team with the most winning players wins. Each win earns one point. After each round of the competition, the team with the most points wins. If the scores of two teams are equal, another final will be required. If the scores of three or more teams are equal, the elimination competition method will be used to determine the championship. It is also heard that the competition date is from 6:00 PM every Monday to Friday, which does not interfere with the occupations of people from all walks of life. For details, you can ask the stadium to read the regulations.

Also, the small football competition at the stadium on October 10th, the game between Chunguang and Wheelock, will be held at 9:30 AM on the 7th (Sunday) in advance.

Shandong Education Adopts New Reforms, Each County Middle School Sets Up Normal School 200

Provincial Normal School Changed to Vocational School

Director of Education He Siyuan Enters Beijing to Ask for Instructions

Jinan Communication, In recent years, the province's 13 provincial middle schools, county middle schools, and private middle schools have established many more. Now, the Shandong Provincial Department of Education is promoting survival education and compulsory education, and setting up normal schools and vocational schools, so that students can learn a skill to make a living after graduation, or serve as teachers in rural primary schools to eliminate illiteracy. It is intended to restrict these surplus county and private junior middle schools. The Ministry of Education has approved the change of each county's middle school to a normal school and the provincial normal school to a vocational school. The reporter met He on the train and asked about everything. According to him, he recently received an order from the Ministry of Education to reform the normal schools, middle schools, and vocational schools in the province, so he entered Beijing to ask for instructions. In addition, he also visited Dean Dai (Chuanxian) to discuss the restoration of the Confucius Temple in Qufu and the preferential treatment of Confucius' descendants. The restoration of the Confucius Temple is a huge project that requires a lot of money. Relying solely on donations will not help. There must be basic funds before one dares to start. Although the general methods for preferential treatment of Confucius' descendants have been drafted, they are also plagued by economic difficulties. All of these need to be discussed with Dean Dai to improve the methods. He is scheduled to return to Jinan from Beijing on the 8th.
